Measures to Reorganize the North China Army Reached 83

The Military Sub-Committee Decided to Cut Troops and Reduce Salaries

Implementation to Begin This Month

Difficulty in Counting Troops, Permitting Self-Reduction

Resolution of the Chahar Incident, Troops Begin to Be Re-Deployed

Beiping Special Dispatch: The war zone has been completely taken over, and the Chahar incident has been largely resolved. The current issues in North China are the reorganization of the army and finances. The reorganization of finances is currently being discussed in detail by Huang Fu and Wang Kemin with the central government. It will not be completely finalized until after the Lushan Conference. Regarding the reorganization of the army, Huang Shaoxiong brought back a reorganization plan from Lushan when he returned north. After discussions between He Yingqin and the various North China generals, the outline has been established. The North China army has undergone repeated changes and is extremely complex. Roughly speaking, it can be divided into the Northeast Army and miscellaneous troops. Before the September 18th Incident, the four provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe had not been lost by the Northeast Army, and the military pay did not entirely come from North China. Only the garrison in the Pass was temporarily within the scope of North China. Since September 18th, the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang have fallen, and Rehe has been entangled. The remaining Northeast Army has gathered in North China, and all the pay has relied entirely on North China for supply. Before the Rehe War, the Northeast Army was organized into brigades. Later, in preparation for war, the brigades were reorganized into divisions, expanding the scope. After the Rehe War, there was a reorganization, divided into three armies, led by Yu Xuezhong, He Guozhao, Wang Yizhe, etc. The number of divisions did not change, only the jurisdiction was slightly adjusted. The number of soldiers in each division was fundamentally insufficient due to the reorganization from brigades, and after the war, it was even more difficult for reality to match the name. However, the payment of military pay remained the same as before and did not change in the slightest. The miscellaneous troops include a wide range, including Shang Zhen's 32nd Army, Song Zheyuan's 29th Army, Sun Dianying's 41st Army, Pang Bingxun's 40th Army, Gao Guizi's 84th Division, and Shen Ke's Provisional First Division. Shang Zhen commanded three divisions: Gao Hongwen, Li Xingcun, and Huang Guanghua. Song Zheyuan originally commanded two divisions: Feng Zhian and Zhang Zizhong. After the Battle of Xifengkou, Zhao Dengyu's division was added. Sun Dianying's troops have recently expanded, in addition to the original 41st Army, incorporating the 55th Army and the Cavalry Army. Pang Bingxun's troops originally had four regiments. Li Fuhe's division of the Northeast Army has also recently been placed under his command. Gao Guizi's troops were originally an independent division. During the Anti-Japanese War, they were temporarily placed under the command of Shang Zhen, and Gao served as Shang's deputy commander-in-chief. Shen Ke's troops were originally under the command of Pang Bingxun, but recently changed to an independent division. During the Anti-Japanese War, each army increased rather than decreased, leading to huge military expenditures. After the war, the local area was dilapidated and finances were difficult. Without reorganization, not only would the organization be complex, but there would be no source for such large military expenditures. Day after day, how could it continue?

During Zhang Xueliang's era, the monthly cost of military pay and clothing for the North China armies was about 7 million. After He Yingqin arrived in Beiping, it was tightened once and reduced to just over 5 million. There was still a large deficit after offsetting income and expenses. When Zhang Xueliang was in charge in Beiping, he could not cope with the situation of having less income than expenses, so he came up with various ways to deduct (1) paying the troops once every thirty-five days, paying only ten times a year, invisibly reducing the pay for two months, (2) the military pay was discounted by 20%, and then discounted again by 20%, eighty-eight is sixty-four, the actual pay was only 64%. With such deductions, it was barely maintained. He Yingqin continued the old rules after coming north, and although it was tightened once, it was still felt that it was difficult to cope. It is now September, and the armies have only been paid four times, with arrears accumulating day by day. Reorganization is imminent.

The reorganization of the army should originally eliminate the weak and retain the strong, carry out practical reorganization, and strictly count the troops for the purpose of downsizing. However, due to the difficulty of reversing the accumulated problems, counting the troops is difficult, and even if there is a desire to count the troops, it is only nominal, and strict reorganization is truly difficult to achieve. We can only deal with it perfunctorily and handle it in a flexible way. Now, after the military sub-committee's deliberation on military pay, it has been decided to implement troop and salary reductions starting this month. The reduction methods are (1) a new establishment will be set, reducing the number of people in each company by more than 30, to be reduced automatically by each army (2) the military sub-committee will verify and reduce military pay, depending on the situation of each army, making reductions of 50,000 to 60,000, 20,000 to 30,000, or even several thousand, with a total reduction of more than 700,000. After such reductions, the monthly reduction can be reduced to just over 4 million, and the difference between income and expenditure is slightly better than before. As for the military sub-committee itself, it is also engaging in personnel cuts and salary reductions to demonstrate thrift. At yesterday's routine meeting of the military sub-committee, it was resolved that all nominal personnel such as consultants and advisers would be changed to honorary positions and salaries would be suspended temporarily.

During the Anti-Japanese War, the armies were mobilized north to kill enemies and defend the country. After the war ended, the Chahar incident arose, and they were unable to return. Now that the Chahar incident has been resolved, the armies are beginning to be demobilized and redeployed. Some of the Central Army that came north has already gone south, and the remaining units will also be demobilized as appropriate. Feng Qinzai's troops will still be transferred back to Shaanxi. Shang Zhen's troops have been ordered to return to the Pinghan Line and garrison between Zhangde and Xuchang. Gao Guizi's troops will be transferred to garrison between Cizhou and Zhengzhou. He Zhuguo's troops will be transferred to garrison around Shijiazhuang and Handan. Each army is currently in the process of being transferred. The large army in the suburbs of Beiping will be transferred elsewhere one after another, gradually returning to normal. (September 7th)

Song Ziwen Attends Lushan Conference 84

Finance Minister Song Reports on Overseas Trip

Key Points of Discussion at the Lushan Conference

Nanchang Dispatch: Finance Minister Song Ziwen arrived in Lushan from Nanjing on the 4th. Details were previously reported. Wang Jingwei and his party arrived at the bay on the Hai Rong warship at around 2 p.m. on the 5th, and immediately transferred to Lushan, arriving at Guling at 5:20 p.m. that day. After Wang and others arrived in Lushan, they began holding meetings that evening at Chiang Kai-shek's residence. Attendees included Chiang Kai-shek, Wang Jingwei, Song Ziwen, Sun Ke, Kong Xiangxi, Tang Youren, Zeng Zhongming, Zou Lin, Chen Shaokuan, Wu Zhihui, Li Shizeng, Zhang Jingjiang, and other members of the Central Committee. First, Finance Minister Song reported on his mission abroad, mainly covering: (1) his participation in economic talks at the invitation of U.S. President Roosevelt, his attendance at the London World Economic Conference, and the signing of the Silver Agreement; (2) his visits to the U.S., Germany, France, Britain, Italy, Belgium, and other countries, where he called on officials of friendly nations; (3) his travels in Europe and America, where he observed politics, military preparations, construction, political parties, and other aspects in various countries. During the meeting, President Wang of the Executive Yuan also reported on central political measures, and Chairman Chiang reported on the national military campaign against the communists. Details of the meeting are not yet known, but according to various sources, the meeting began with Finance Minister Song's report, which will serve as a reference for policy implementation. In addition, regarding (1) diplomacy with Japan and the aftermath of the North China war zone, specific policies will be determined after Huang Fu arrives; (2) the current Yellow River flood situation is serious, and detailed measures for Yellow River water management and rural relief will be decided at this meeting; (3) the communist suppression in five provinces and the elimination of communist bandits in Sichuan, Hubei, and Hunan are the most critical factors for the country's stability. Chairman Chiang is determined to use the nation's military, financial, and human resources to contain this source of chaos. Regarding post-disaster relief in the five provinces, there will be practical and fundamental measures for both short-term and long-term political funding. Furthermore, the revitalization and improvement of internal affairs, the consolidation and development of finance, and other matters will also be discussed in detail. It is reported that the conference will only last for two or three days and is intended as a conversational exchange of views. The results of the discussions will be brought back to Nanjing by Wang and Song and submitted to the central government for implementation. The most important aspect is to use the new spirit that Song brought back from Europe and America as the key element for improving everything. (September 7th)

Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission Formulates Yellow River Management Plan 85

Divided into Three Engineering Projects: Closing Breaches, Repairing Dams, and Strengthening Dikes

Jinan Dispatch: Regarding the overall plan for managing the Yellow River in Hebei, Shandong, and Henan, the flood prevention conference has decided to entrust the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission to take charge. The commission plans to establish temporary engineering offices in the three provinces immediately to actively carry out construction. Xu Xinwu, a member of the commission, and engineers Wang Fengjae and Lu Keming arrived in Jinan yesterday and paid a visit to Chairman Han today to discuss construction methods. Han expressed strong support for their plan. Xu spoke in detail to reporters about the specific plans for managing the Yellow River, which are recorded as follows:

Temporary Engineering Offices to be Established in Various Provinces 86

Xu said, "I departed from Bian on the 3rd of this month, passing through Lanfeng, Kaocheng, Zhengzhou, Wenxian, Wuzhi, Rongze, and other places along the way, observing the situation. I arrived in Jinan via Xuzhou. After consulting with the provincial governments regarding the aftermath of the Yellow River, the commission will implement the plan. Because the Yellow River flood this time has affected several provinces, the Huai River Conservancy Commission and the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission from Hebei, Shandong, Henan, Jiangsu, Anhui, and Shaanxi have gathered together to discuss flood prevention issues. As a result, the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission has been entrusted with the management of the Yellow River. After receiving this commission, we have drafted methods for handling the aftermath of the Yellow River and will establish temporary engineering offices in the provinces affected by the flood. The first district will be located in Kaifeng, Henan; the second in Changyuan, Hebei; and the third in Heze, Shandong. The first district has already been established. My purpose in coming to Shandong this time is to discuss with Chairman Han the establishment of the third district's temporary engineering office. Then I will go to Hebei to discuss the methods for the third district's engineering office. The principle of the commission's management of the Yellow River this time is to cooperate with the provincial governments. The heads of the engineering offices in each district will be concurrently held by the directors of the river affairs bureaus of the respective provinces. The heads will manage the administration, and the engineers from the commission will manage the engineering. The head of the Henan engineering office is Chen Ruzhen, the director of the river affairs bureau, and the engineer is Cai Lianggong. The engineer for the second district is Wang Fengjae, and the engineer for the third district in Shandong is planned to be Lu Keming. Although the three districts are divided according to provinces this time, they are not strictly defined, in order to facilitate the work."

Funding and Steps of Work 87

The commission has formulated three steps for managing the Yellow River: (1) Closing the breaches; (2) Repairing dams at dangerous points; (3) Repairing the main dikes. The work is not very difficult, but funding is a major issue. The Executive Yuan has allocated 500,000 yuan for emergency projects, but in reality, 500,000 yuan is far from enough. Therefore, the flood prevention conference has resolved to allocate 10 million yuan for Yellow River management projects. However, this is just a request from the flood prevention conference, and it is not yet known whether it can be achieved. When I was leaving Beijing, I visited President Wang, and President Wang promised to allocate 500,000 yuan to cope with the first phase of the project, with subsequent allocations to follow. Therefore, while closing the breaches to meet the demands of the people, we are also planning to repair the dams. We will do as much as we can depending on how much funding the central government allocates. Because the commission is responsible for the technical aspects, we are planning ahead. In addition to planning to close the breaches first, we are also planning the entire river project. If more funds continue to be allocated, the project will continue. Regarding this point, Chairman Han of this province also advocates closing the breaches first and then repairing the entire river, which is the same view. There are many dangerous points along the upper and lower reaches of the Yellow River. If adequate funds are available, proper repairs can be made to avoid danger. Otherwise, there is a possibility of danger occurring every year due to major floods.

Lanfeng and Zhengzhou are Most Important 88

Regarding the breach situation, I have seen it in Henan. (1) The Lanfeng breach is a levee breach. (2) The Kaocheng breach is a scour breach. (3) At the north bank of Zhengzhou, the local area has already closed a part of it. (4) The Wenxian levee breach is 50 li long. Closing the Kaocheng and Lanfeng breaches is not difficult, but the East Dam project is important. Western Shandong and northern Jiangsu are in danger of being damaged. The topography there is that the Yellow River comes from the west, and at the head of the East Dam in Lanfeng, it turns north in a large bend and then flows east. West of the East Dam, there is an old breach, which is the old Yellow River. The constructed dike is called the New Dike. East of the head of the East Dam, there is a gap in the main dike that has not been closed. North of the dike there is a ring dike, and north of the ring dike there is a people's dike. The breach this time was caused by the floodwater coming from the north to the south, first overflowing the people's dike, traveling south for 20 li, then breaching the ring dike, flowing out from the old gap in the main dike, and flooding Kaocheng. According to common sense, river water that overflows a people's dike and travels 20 li would not have much force. Unexpectedly, the force of the water this time was so great, which is shocking. Therefore, in terms of the situation, it is easy to close the Lanfeng breach, but to avoid the danger in western Shandong and northern Jiangsu, the East Dam project is very important. Furthermore, regarding the Zhengzhou project, the Yellow River Railway Bridge spans the river. The southern end is on the south bank of the river, and the northern end is built on the old river beach. According to the chief of the Pinghan Railway section, before the accident, the main current was close to the south bank, with a depth of more than 30 zhang. Unexpectedly, within 24 hours, the main current shifted to the north bank, and the south bank silted up into a large beach, 7 li away from the south bank. The main current shifted north and breached the dike, flowing north from Zhan Dian. The local people then tore open the railway to avoid being flooded. Many persuasions could not stop them. In terms of the situation here, closing the breach is not very difficult, but strengthening the north bank is very important. If it is breached, the river water may seize the Wei River and change its course to the sea. North China will suffer an unprecedented major flood. The above situation is of great importance and is a national issue, not a local one.

Repairing Dams at Various Dangerous Points 89

The Lanfeng East Dam and the Pinghan Railway Bridge are all very important. The river dams should be repaired immediately. In Hebei, there is one breach at the south bank and 32 large and small breaches within 70 li on the north bank. The interests are all related to Shandong. Therefore, the breach closing project is most burdensome in Hebei, followed by Henan. In addition, there are many places along the river where dams need to be repaired. Furthermore, the entire dike needs to be repaired because low dikes are prone to overflowing and thin dikes are prone to being breached. Therefore, they must be raised and thickened to ensure safety. The above projects are just planned in this way. Whether they can be achieved depends entirely on the central government's financial resources.

Han of Shandong Endorses This Plan 90

After Xu and others visited Han, reporters visited again. At that time, Zhang Lianjia, director of the Shandong River Affairs Bureau, was discussing engineering issues with Xu and others. Wang Yaodan received them. According to him, the purpose of visiting Han was to seek Han's opinion on this plan and to request the transfer of Director Zhang (Lianjia) to be the head of the third district's engineering office and to transfer river workers from Shandong Province to work in the third district. Han not only expressed strong support for this but had no other comments. He also strongly supported the transfer of Shandong river workers and immediately appointed Director Zhang to discuss the current engineering issues with us in detail. The main engineering project to be undertaken in the third district is the repair and closure of the breach at Erfen Zhuang. The engineering office can be established within two or three days and begin collecting materials. Once the materials are collected, the repair work will begin immediately. The principle of this district's project is that the central government will allocate funds and Shandong will provide personnel. Chairman Han and Director Zhang have both stated that it is very good and advocated that it should be done as quickly as possible. (6th)

Yellow River Breach Closure to Begin This Month 91

Regarding the construction methods for closing the breach, according to Wang Xi today, the Yellow River breach has not been closed for more than a month. The river water is flowing out vigorously, and the water in the disaster area has increased rather than decreased. Most of the victims are trapped in the water, and all relief efforts are difficult to carry out. Moreover, winter is approaching, and relief will be even more difficult. It will not be easy to close the breach in the cold weather. Therefore, the only urgent task now is to close the breach. After we arrived in Jinan, we contacted the local officials several times and decided that the south bank of the Erfen Zhuang breach (the breach is actually at Xiao Pang Zhuang, east of Erfen Zhuang) will be closed by the third district. Because Changyuan County there belongs to Hebei Province, Commissioner Xu (Xinwu) will go to Tianjin tomorrow to discuss the security of the construction area with Chairman Yu. Today, Xu discussed with Zhang Honglie, director of the Construction Department of Shandong, and Zhang Lianjia, director of the River Affairs Bureau, and decided that Director Zhang, Lu (Keming), and I will go to Dongming Erfen Zhuang in two or three days to survey the project. I am responsible for the engineering affairs of the second district, so I will cross the river from Erfen Zhuang to the north bank to prepare everything. Regarding the engineering issues of the second district, I have already contacted Sun Qingze, director of the Hebei River Affairs Bureau. Therefore, I will go to Batou Town in Changyuan County in three or four days to organize the engineering office. The first step in closing the breach is to conduct an on-site survey, estimate the amount of materials needed, purchase them, and then organize the engineering office to supervise the work. The Erfen Zhuang breach is one kilometer wide and has no main current, so closing the breach should not be difficult. The north bank has 32 large and small breaches with a total width of more than 3 kilometers. If materials are purchased from western Shandong, it will be difficult because western Shandong has been flooded, and it will also be difficult to transport them upstream by boat. Therefore, it has been decided to purchase materials near Lanfeng. The materials needed are mainly sorghum stalks, and the old method will still be used to close the breach. The temporary engineering office of the third district will be located in Jinan in the future. The office was originally planned to be located in Heze, but now it has been moved to Gao Zhuang because Heze is far from the work area. Construction can begin in one month, and it is hoped that the closure can be completed by the end of the year to complete the first phase of the plan. The project cost is currently 20,000 yuan. (7th)

Impressions of the Swedish Prince's Visit to China 92

Great Interest in Visiting Beiping, Praises Kaihua Paper as Comparable to Swedish Paper,盛称故宫建築偉大華茶亟應加以改良北平特訉Great Praise for the Great Architecture of the Forbidden City, Chinese Tea Urgently Needs to be Improved.

Beiping Special Dispatch: Prince Carl of Sweden has been in Beiping for several days, and his interest in sightseeing and touring is very strong. As of today (7th), he has visited Zhongshan Park, Taimiao, the Temple of Heaven, the Confucius Temple, the Imperial College, Yonghe Temple, Beihai Park, the Summer Palace, the Great Wall, and also visited the National Beiping Library, the Relics Exhibition Hall, the Three Great Halls, the Museum of History, the Palace Museum, and attended banquets hosted by He Yingqin, acting chairman of the Military Branch, and Yuan Liang, mayor of Beiping. Prince Carl's interest in visiting Beiping is stronger than in any other place. The reporter specially interviewed Prince Carl, and the main points of the conversation are as follows:

The Glory of Chinese Paper 93

This time I came to China because I have long admired Chinese cultural monuments, so I came to visit, completely as an individual tourist to admire the scenery, study academic knowledge, and examine the beautiful customs and cultural systems of China, and I do not represent the Swedish government and have absolutely no mission. The Chinese paper industry was originally very developed. As far as I know, Cai Lun of the Han Dynasty invented paper, using tree bark, hemp heads, old cloth, and fishing nets as paper. The world called it Cai Hou Paper, which shows that the Chinese paper industry had inventions thousands of years before paper was used in Europe. During the Qianlong era of the Qing Dynasty, Kaihua paper reached its peak. In the middle of the Qing Dynasty, Lian Si paper was cheap and required less labor, so Kaihua paper became an antique. Because China invented paper the earliest, ancient culture was also very early. Modern papermaking in Sweden is quite developed. Although the quality of the paper is excellent, the fineness of the materials is not as good as that of Chinese Kaihua paper. Swedish paper is the best in Europe and can print five-color overprints. Europeans all say that Chinese paper cannot print five-color paintings, only use colored painting. But that's not true. The temple block books I saw in the Palace Museum in Beiping were printed on Kaihua paper, and their five-color pictures were completely printed on the whitest Kaihua paper, and they have not faded for hundreds of years and are as bright as newly painted. Its printing method uses one side of the paper, which is different from the two-sided printing of Swedish paper. Two-sided printing is certainly more economical, but if the printed book is out of print, it will be harmed on both sides if it encounters stupid insects. If one side of the Chinese paper is used for printing, only one side will be damaged when it encounters stupid insects, which is also an advantage of Chinese paper. If printing newspapers, Swedish paper is still the best, one because of two-sided printing, and two because the paper is thicker. If Chinese papermaking is improved, it will join hands with the Swedish paper industry in the future to jointly promote the development of the paper industry and promote Eastern and Western culture, which is a valuable undertaking.

Page 14

Representative of Ancient Culture 94

My brothers and sisters have all come to China. (The Swedish Royal Family) Five or six years ago, 余 talked about Chinese industry and commerce. Today, Chinese industry and commerce have indeed made considerable progress compared to five or six years ago. Zhongshan 　in Nanjing, East and West Chang'an Streets and Fuyou Street in Beiping all have new black roads, and railroad transfers are also better than before. It is expected that there will be even greater progress in the future. Beiping is the ancient capital of the Chinese emperors of the past dynasties. Various buildings contain the meaning of Eastern art. The architecture of the Forbidden City is larger than the Swedish Royal Palace. Although some of the antiques stored in the palaces have been transported to the south, there are still many that have not been transported. I have a few eye blessings to visit. In short, Beiping can represent the ancient Chinese style of culture. There are many empty spaces in Nanjing. The National Government has established its capital in Nanjing, and all construction projects are just beginning. Nanjing can represent the modern Chinese style of civilization. Ancient culture should be preserved, and modern civilization should also be developed. The Chinese people love peace. Although there are disadvantages, most countries in the world sympathize with China. The people of Sweden are also very peaceful. The country has been peaceful and prosperous for decades. Although it is in the midst of the European panic, Sweden is not affected. There are fewer unemployed people in the country than in other countries. China is in this chaotic world and has not been greatly affected by it. The people of both countries can be proud of this. Although our industry and commerce are gradually developing, there are not many industrial and commercial interests in Beiping, so there is no minister in Beiping. All matters are handled by the Swedish Chargé d'Affaires or Consul General in Shanghai, but I hope that Swedish industry and commerce will develop in China and that ministers will be added in the future to coexist and prosper with China.

Jiang and Song are Special Talents 95

I believe that China is currently in a period of evolution, and the future prospects are unlimited. For example, Chairman Chiang (Kai-shek) and Minister Song (Ziwen) are both special talents in China's military and economy. The National Government also has full governing power. Your country is located in the East Asian continent, rich in resources, and industry and commerce are striving for progress. Sweden is located in northern Western Europe. Although the national territory is not as large as China, due to geographical relations, it has made great efforts in industry and national defense. The world is wrongly praised, and many say that our country's industry is comparable to the United States, and weapons are even superior to Germany. This kind of words is enough to encourage our country to work harder in national defense and industry. Most of China's natural treasures have not been exploited. In the future, many countries in the world will rely on your country. Our country is located in the far north of Europe, close to the frigid zone, and the climate is extremely cold. People are mostly resistant to cold and are proficient in skiing and skating. Every summer, there is sunlight day and night. When sleeping at night, most people cover the windows with curtains to avoid the sun shining in. In winter, you can only see four hours of sunlight a day, which is not common in temperate countries. I hope that the reporters will visit our country, and I will welcome you. I am now working on economic research and will engage in commercial development in the future. I hope to exchange well-known Swedish paper and steel for Chinese native products such as soybeans, tea, and silk.

Sweden Welcomes Chinese Tea 96

The people of our country welcome your country's tea very much, but in recent years, various countries have also promoted tea planting, which has greatly hit Chinese tea, and the tea planted in a certain country in the East mostly pretends to be Chinese tea for sale, confusing the fish with the pearls, which is chilling. In fact, the one that is welcome in Sweden is still the real Chinese tea. I am now scheduled to leave Ping for Tianjin on the 9th, and will only stay in Tianjin for a few hours before going to Qingdao. I will only stay in Qingdao for a short time before going to Shanghai. Shanghai is the center of China's economy and has long been famous in the world. Although it has been ravaged by a certain country, I believe that it can achieve the hope of revival in the shortest time. I will leave Shanghai on the 29th and may go to Hankou before returning to Sweden. (7th Jin)

He Chengjun Inspects Various Districts in Eastern Hubei 97

Reviewing Troops Along the Way and Soliciting Public Opinion

A Military Conference Was Convened After Arriving at Songbu

Zhang Qun and His Party Returned to Hubei by Car from Hunan

Hankou Dispatch: He Chengjun, the Pacification Commissioner of Hubei, departed from Hankou by car at 10 a.m. on the 7th to inspect eastern Hubei. The accompanying personnel included senior staff officer Xu Chengxi, staff officer Chen Yucang, adjutant Zhao Yixue, Wang Renshan, Cheng Ruhai, administrative commissioner of the Fourth District, and Chen Shuzi, director of the 13th Division's office in Hankou. The garrison commander and garrison brigade commander Ye Peng also personally led a machine gun company and a special service platoon to escort him. He talked about the tasks of this trip before the journey: (1) Inspect the situation of the aftermath in the recovered bandit areas; (2) Deeply into the countryside to inquire about the sufferings of the people; (3) Investigate the military discipline and style of the stationed troops; (4) Confer with the generals to wipe out the remaining bandits and instruct them on the appropriate measures. He's car arrived in Huangpi at 12 noon. The army brigade commander Liu Yifeng, the county magistrate Hua Wenxuan, and representatives of the people greeted him ten li away. He successively summoned officers and soldiers of the special service brigade and public groups to give speeches, and then proceeded to Qiting. Ye Peng returned to Hankou from Huangpi because the security of Wuhan was important. It was heard that after He arrived in Qiting, he inspected Zhang Liansan's troops and ordered them to quickly move to the new defense area in southern Hubei. He then went to Songbu to convene a military conference for the bandit suppression generals. It is reported that General Commander Sun Lianzhong and Division Commander Wan Yaohuang, and Peng Zhensan have arrived in Songbu to welcome him. Both Army Commander Shangguan Yunxiang and Army Commander Hao Mengling arrived in Macheng and will go to Songbu to attend the meeting. He will leave Songbu to inspect the counties of Songma after the meeting is held, and will return to Hankou within a week. When He left Hankou, Zhang Qun was returning to Hubei from Hunan. Zhang and Construction Director Li Fanyi, Education Director Cheng Qibao, departed from Wuchang on the 1st and arrived in Changsha on the 2nd, and then discussed the aftermath of the bandit area in southern Hubei with Commander-in-Chief He Jian in detail. Both the problems of cooperation for water conservancy in Xiang and E were resolved and specific plans were determined, and they also visited various constructions and traveled to famous places such as Nanyue and Yuelu. On the 6th, Zhang and the two directors Li and Cheng returned to Hubei on a special express train on the Xiang-E Road. At 8 a.m. on the 7th, they arrived in Wuchang. At 12 noon on the same day, the provincial government convened a meeting to discuss the post-disaster plan for western Hubei. It was decided to formally propose the plan to the provincial government's regular meeting on the 8th for implementation. (7th)

Palace Museum Has Been Taken Over 98

Yi Peiji Did Not Attend Due to Illness, Represented by Wu Ying

Yuan Liang's Inventory Will Take About a Month to Complete

Beiping Special Dispatch: The issue of the takeover of the Palace Museum is quite complicated. The new acting director Ma Heng exchanged opinions with the former director Yi Peiji beforehand. After the principles and methods were stipulated, the takeover began in two parts on the 6th. The situation of each party is recorded as follows:

Takeover Situation 99

At 9 a.m. on the 6th, the new acting director Ma Heng and the inventory committee member Yuan Liang arrived at the museum one after another. The takeover committee members Wang Shiduo, Yu Heyin, Zhuang Shangyan (Wu Yu Zhang on behalf), Yu Gai, He Chengyi, Li Yihua (Duan Qiongchu on behalf), Huang Pengxiao (Shan Shikui on behalf), Wang Meizhuang, Dong Yinfu, Cheng Zushao, Li Xiuda, Dai Zengpei, Su Yongzhong, and the handover committee members Yu Tongkui, Wu Ying, Zhou Shinan, Yu Heyin, Xu Wenzhen, Cheng Runtang, and others also arrived at the museum on time. The former director Yi Peiji did not attend due to illness and was represented by Secretary Wu Ying. At about 10 a.m., the personnel of the two committees, the handover and takeover committees, and the new director Ma Heng held a joint meeting and began to discuss the handover procedures. After the ceremony, the takeover of the two parts was carried out: (1) The administrative part was completed on the 6th. (2) The item part. Because the number was too large, one part was handed over every day. The method of random inspection was used. The inventory committee member Yuan Liang, who was very busy due to government affairs, expressed at the meeting that he was responsible for supervising all the procedures of the handover on the orders of the Executive Yuan. Regarding whether there was any corruption in the handover of various affairs and items, he could be responsible for exposing it. Yuan left after sitting for a while and then sent Wang Yu Kui, chief of the first section of the municipal government, to represent him, supervisor and committee member can attend the meeting before taking over the items. The item part was officially accepted on the 6th. There was no time limit set for the handover. It should take about one month to complete.

Consultation Process 100

After the board of directors of the Palace Museum approved the resignation of Director Yi Peiji and Secretary-General Li Zongtong, Ma Heng was appointed as acting director. At that time, Ma was in the Beijing-Shanghai area and sent a telegram to Xu Hongbao to be the secretary-general. After Xu arrived at the museum to take office, he discussed the takeover matters with Wu Ying, the former secretary of the Palace Museum, several times. Wu repeatedly asked the former director Yi Peiji for instructions. As a result, the new and old parties agreed on the takeover method. Yi organized a handover committee and Ma organized a takeover committee. When Ma returned to Ping, this principle had been completely determined. Ma also considered the actual situation with all parties and decided to start the takeover on September 6th. For items that were inventoried, those with draft books would be neatly transcribed, and those with inventories would be handed over according to the inventories. If there were items that were transferred between the archives, antiquities, and library, they must be returned to the original archive before they can be handed over. The daily office hours were stipulated, and the responsible personnel from both sides went to the museum to work on time. If it could not be completed in one month, it would be extended.

Reorganization Methods 101

The method of changing the organization of the Palace Museum is that the Executive Yuan first formulates the principles and then hands them over to the Legislative Yuan to draft. These principles have already been internally decided, and the detailed content has not yet been announced, so the public announcement is temporarily delayed. Therefore, it is of course necessary to change the various organizations at this time. A part of the valuable antiquities has already been transported south in five batches. Now that the situation in the north has stabilized, some of these antiquities must be transported back, and some must be kept in the south. The antiquities kept in the south will be displayed in the Nanjing branch when it is established. As for how to allocate the antiquities, it will be discussed at the next board meeting. However, since the Palace Museum has a branch, there will naturally be changes in the organization. (7th Jin)

Fatal Electrocution of Telephone Worker in Songjiang 102

Yesterday (the 7th) at 7:30 PM, an electric light wire near the tax police training center at Dong School Field in this city suddenly snapped and fell onto a telephone line, cutting off telephone service to the training center and causing thick smoke and occasional sparks to erupt from the switchboard inside the telephone company's central office. Personnel were dispatched to investigate and, after determining the situation, immediately notified the electric light company to temporarily shut off the circuit. Five workers were sent to repair the line. As it was nighttime, the telephone workers assumed the circuit had been shut off and there was no danger. They proceeded to disentangle the broken electric light wire from the telephone wire. Unexpectedly, the circuit had not been shut off, and the broken cable fell, striking telephone worker Hu Huigen. Hu fell to the ground. Another worker, Wu Ahe, seeing this, rushed to help and was also electrocuted and fell. Another worker used a wooden board to push the electric wire away. Two workers on the utility pole, witnessing their comrades' tragic deaths, were so frightened that they fell and injured their backs. The training center then notified the telephone company, and the dead and injured workers were taken to Songjiang Hospital. Except for Hu and Wu, whose bodies were charred beyond saving, the two injured workers were not in mortal danger. After the telephone workers' tragic deaths, the electric light company finally sent workers. The training center had notified the company three times, but the workers arrived only after a long delay, leading to this disaster. Responsibility is clearly assigned, and two electric light workers have been temporarily detained.

Suzhou and Jiangyin to Soon Establish Airfields 103

Xu Ligeng, leader of the aerial photography team of the Aviation Survey Unit of the General Staff Headquarters, flew to Suzhou in the Survey No. 2 aircraft. The surveying of flight routes has already been noted in this newspaper. That night, Xu and his team stayed at the Dongwu Hotel outside the Changmen gate. A reporter visited them. According to Xu, they had recently returned from Nanchang, having first gone to a location in Anhui Province to establish a fortress. However, because the terrain near Jiangyin was considered more important, they were ordered by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to go there. Since there was no airfield near Jiangyin, they stopped in Suzhou. Furthermore, because they were ordered to depart in haste, they had not been able to notify the local airfield in advance, so there were no preparations. As a result, the plane's wheels were caught in the weeds upon landing. Xu had initially thought that the Suzhou airfield would have oil and a protection team, but these were lacking. Therefore, after landing, he immediately contacted the county government to request assistance and arranged for water police to provide protection. He also personally funded the hiring of laborers to remove the weeds from the airfield, with a deadline of [the] 8th to complete the work. He had already entrusted the Meifu Petroleum Company's Shanghai agent with providing the needed oil. If everything can be completed as scheduled today, [the] 9th, they can take off and begin work. Xu also mentioned that the aircraft was a [blank], so even though there was no [blank] in the airfield, parking in the open air was not a problem. At [blank] time, pilot Zhu Daxian, an Indian, returned from outside. Xu immediately pointed him out to the reporter, saying that during the January 28th Incident, pilot Zhu had shot down two Japanese aircraft. Zhu had also been injured in the left waist, and still had a scar. The reporter expressed his admiration for Zhu.

National Goods Exhibition Hall Opens Today 104

The National Goods Exhibition Hall, organized by the Wuxian County Chamber of Commerce, has been in preparation for six months. Over 5,000 various national goods have been collected. The location is at the original site of the Chamber of Commerce Corps headquarters on West Baihua Lane. Preparations have been completed, and the opening ceremony will be held this morning (the 9th). Various national goods factories have prepared various products to be given to the guests as a symbol of promotion.

Wujiang County Government Executes Three Notorious Bandits 105

The three notorious bandits, Chen Fantong (aka Xu Jinfeng), Zhang Zhiqiang, and Gao Desheng (aka Xiao Gao), who had previously robbed ships on the Suzhou-Wujiang route and kidnapped a female hostage from Henglu Town in the two counties of Wuxian and Wujiang, and killed Wang Wenxiang, a detective from the Third District of the Waterborne Provincial Public Security Bureau, etc., were captured by the Wuxian County Police Team. The [blank] Water Patrol Team dispatched police to escort the three criminals to the county government for interrogation. They confessed to their crimes, and a detailed request was sent to the provincial government for approval to execute them. Yesterday (the 7th) at 8:00 AM, the county government received a telegram from the provincial government ordering the execution. Secretary Tong Mingxin identified the three criminals, tied them up, and took them outside the East Gate for execution.

Emergency Meeting of All County Butchers 106

The butchers of this county, oppressed by the tax collectors of slaughter tax, convened an emergency meeting of all the butchers of the county on the afternoon of the 5th at the Wujiang County Chamber of Commerce. (1) It was resolved that Tang Shouyi, which is a pseudonym for Tang Jizhi, who claims to be handling the special construction donation of this county, is not recognized. All special donations due for the seventh and eighth months shall be collected by each district and submitted to the guild, which will then forward them to the Chamber of Commerce to be paid to the county. (2) Tang Shouyi's handling of the slaughter tax, while not increasing the bid price this time, has illegally increased taxes. A letter shall be sent to the County Chamber of Commerce to be forwarded to the Education Funds Management Office to request the removal of the collector to alleviate the merchants' difficulties. (3) If the Education Funds Management Office does not provide a satisfactory response, a complete business shutdown will be implemented to show their determination.

Additional Problems Arise in Wuxi Principal's Lawsuit 107

Qin Zhizhong, the principal of the privately established Peixi Primary School outside Ximen in this county, was suddenly accused by Zhang Baiyun and others to the provincial government last month. Later, additional problems arose when Yu Zengyuan, a citizen of the Western District, published an advertisement stating that Qin Zhizhong's appointment as principal of the school was due to the use of him by Li Guozhang, a teacher at the school. Because Li Guozhang had previously been ordered to never be employed again and did not have the qualifications of a principal, he had to use a false name. In reality, the full authority of the school was completely in Li's hands. Now, Principal Qin was suffering for others and those who levied exorbitant taxes were still in office, etc. After seeing the report, Li also published a rebuttal and described his achievements in running the school. He also filed a defamation lawsuit against Yu Zengyuan in the criminal court of the county court. Yesterday, Judge Lai Sihu ruled that Yu Zengyuan was sentenced to two months in prison, suspended for two years, and ordered the entire verdict to be published in the newspaper. After hearing the verdict, Yu Zengyuan, feeling angry, went straight to the Santai Rice Shop outside the Ximen shed and met with Yang Zhongzi, a school director of Peixi School. He requested that the board of directors meeting be convened to replace Li Guozhang. Because Yang could not agree to this immediately, Yu jumped into the river at Ximen Bridge in an attempt to end his life. Fortunately, he was pulled out of the water, but he had become a drowned chicken. Yu sat blankly on the shore, talking eloquently about his willingness to fight to the end for Peixi and sacrifice his life to express his heart. He had now lost the lawsuit and could not afford to appeal because the expenses required for the last hearing had been covered by pawning clothes for one dollar. Those who heard about it sighed in regret. Then, Yang Zhongzi agreed to convene a board of directors meeting to resolve the matter, and Yu knelt down and thanked him before leaving.

Major Flood Disaster in Chongming's Fifth District 108

The Fifth District of Chongming County, located in the east, is relatively low-lying. On the night of the second of this month, a strong wind suddenly arose, and a flash flood occurred. The coastal dikes were completely breached. The water was more than ten feet deep on the plains, and almost all thatched huts were submerged. The number of people and animals drowned is unknown. The entire Fifth District has largely become a swamp. The eastern and southern coasts were less affected, and the northern coast was the worst. On the night of the third, the flood returned, and even those who had taken refuge in high places on the northern coast suffered deaths and injuries. Such a huge disaster has never occurred before. Now, grief is everywhere, the people are starving and displaced, and their cries fill the air. It is heart-wrenching to hear and even more heartbreaking to witness. The Fifth District Office and other organizations have formed a flood relief committee to find ways to provide relief.

Bandit Activity Resurges in Nantong's Rural Areas 109

Bandits have been actively causing trouble in the four rural areas of Nantong recently. According to reports, the county government, believing that bandits in the rural areas were attempting to seize police and militia firearms, ordered all districts on the 7th to implement joint defense and strengthen security. Regarding the scattered bandits along the Yangtze River and the sea, the Fourth District of the Water Police Department dispatched troops to suppress them.

Military Firearm Cache Case in Shazhou 110

Feng Ziyun, the bandit involved in the military firearm cache case discovered in Changyin Shazhou, has been executed. Huang Wanrong and others, who were accomplices, are being interrogated by the court. Recently, the county government also arrested Cui Xilin, a key criminal in the case. Due to the serious nature of the case, a special request has been made to the court to review the records and investigate it.

Bandits Rob and Injure People in Rugao's Jiangyuan Township 111

Yao Wenxiang's house in Jiangyuan Township, Baipu District, was suddenly attacked by a number of bandits carrying flashlights and firearms around 11:00 PM on the 3rd. Speaking with foreign accents, they forced their way inside, tied up and beat the owner, and also tied up the owner's third son and threw him into the river. It is estimated that they robbed away many pieces of silver, clothes, jewelry, and cloth. The loss was huge. The owner has reported the incident to the district militia headquarters, which has forwarded it to the county government, and they have dispatched personnel to investigate and pursue the stolen goods.

Jiangyin Strictly Investigates the Embezzlement of Opium Case 112

Min Weizhi, the squad leader of the First Squad of the County Police Team stationed at the old seawall in Shazhou, and Yuan Haichou and Chen Yan, inspectors of the Waterborne Police stationed there, colluded with shipowner Song Lao Si and others on July 22nd around 7:00 PM in the embezzlement of a large quantity of opium. After investigation and verification by the County Supervisory Committee, Min Weizhi and shipowner Song Lao Si, who was already in custody, were summoned to the county government on the 4th for interrogation. The shipowner clearly confessed that there were two [blank] and one vat of opium, weighing more than 3,000 taels, and that there were actually one to two hundred catties of opium. Min Weizhi was taken into custody. Chen Yan was on the run but was apprehended in Jingjiang Sidunzi on the 6th and was escorted to the county on the 7th by Squad Leader Shen for confrontation with Min Weizhi. After interrogation, he was taken into custody. Because of this case, it was suspected that Chen Yan had been falsely accused by Pan Zhushan, a local person, and reported to the district office. Pan refused to accept this and appealed to the public [blank] requesting the county to summon him for interrogation. It has been scheduled for interrogation on the coming [blank] day.

Intense Gunfight Between Police and Bandits in Gaoyou's Putuan Village 113

A number of bandits suddenly came to Putuan Village in the Ninth District of this county a few days ago. Each of them was armed with firearms and intended to loot the village. This was detected by the police team stationed in Xinzhuang, who came to arrest them. They exchanged fire with the bandits in an intense gunfight that lasted two hours. It is estimated that two bandits were killed and one was injured. The bandits, unable to resist, fled to the southeast.

Guo Ju Township Suffers Second Incident of Bandit Arson and Looting 114

The homes of farmers Yan Yonghe, Xue Zhirong, Gao Ruixia, Mei Hongkuan, and others in Guo Ju Township, Fourth District of the county, as well as the homes of Guangrong and Zhou Guangtai in Bai Zhou Ma Town, were simultaneously robbed by bandits last month. Mei Hongkuan's wife, Yan, and four others were kidnapped and a large ransom was demanded. After repeated negotiations, due to the wide disparity in the ransom price, they were unable to redeem them. Unexpectedly, the bandits went to Guo Ju Township again a few days ago, looted everything, and burned down Yan Yonghe's residence, declaring that if the ransom was not paid, they would come and kill everyone in the village.

Zhenjiang Police Chief, a European, Accused 115

Wang Weijun, the son of Wang Muzhan, an official of the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department, was watching a sporting event at the public stadium a few days ago. Because he was not maintaining order, he was punched and injured by Bu Zhenhai, the police chief of Zhenjiang County. Weijun cried bitterly at the time. Later, relatives rushed to the scene and took him back. His father, hearing of this, was unwilling to accept it and hired Fang Hao, a lawyer, to file a private prosecution with the court. The court hearing was yesterday. The defendant, Bu Zhenhai, did not appear. Only the plaintiff, Wang Muzhan, and his son Weijun were summoned and interrogated. It was ordered that the defendant be arrested and brought before the court for further investigation.

Yangzhou Granary Officials Collude in Fraud Case 116

Han Jiandong and other villagers in the Seventh District of this county filed a complaint accusing Liu Huancheng, the chief clerk of the Second Granary, and Guo Xichun, the supervising collector, of colluding in fraud and illegally collecting money and grain from disaster-stricken areas. In addition to the party and government jointly dispatching special investigators to thoroughly investigate the matter, County Magistrate Ma personally interrogated them. The false collusion of three households, Xu Youfu, was discovered. On the 6th, witnesses were summoned again for further interrogation. Over twenty people, including the plaintiffs, defendants, witnesses, and households who had made false statements, arrived and were interrogated one by one. According to the households who had made false statements, the false statements were given by the grain clerks who came to their doors. They did not reveal exactly who they were, only saying that they recognized the false statement but did not recognize the person who gave the money. The defendant denied the false statements and claimed that the twenty years of forced labor were collected before the disaster registration was received. The debate was fierce. After five hours of interrogation, due to the complexity of the situation, no results were obtained.

Jingjiang Fourth Branch Station Patrol Officer Removed from Post 117

Liu Zhengbao, a patrol officer at the Gushan Town Public Security Fourth Branch Station, was dismissed from his post by the county government and investigated by the County Public Security Bureau for illegally detaining brothers Zhu Wangtong and Zhu Tongsheng, villagers, after their father, Guan Song, complained to the county. Wu Yanzhang has been temporarily appointed to replace him.

Jiashan-Shanghai Boat Robbery Case Solved 118

The robbery of the Shanghai-Hangzhou liner in Jiashan has been the subject of much discussion. The case was finally solved yesterday. The robber was Wang Bamei, a famous female bandit from Pudong, Jiangzhe. This female bandit was unusually strong and fierce, roaming the Jiangzhe area and invincible. This time, she conspired with her paramour, bandit Shi, to rob the boat. Bandit Shi had 30-40 followers and three ships. After the robbery, they scattered into the Dianshan Lake area. After the Qingpu County Water Police cooperated with the county police team to suppress them, the notorious bandit Wang Bamei was captured yesterday. She was transferred to the Su-Song Bandit Suppression Command for interrogation that night. As for the whereabouts of bandit Shi, there are clues and his arrest is certain in the coming days.

Hangzhou Firewood Vendor Commits Suicide by Poison After Being Swindled 119

Qian Shuangfu, a 50-year-old firewood vendor living at No. 3 Ruyi Lane, west of the Gongchen Bridge in Hangzhou, supported himself by selling firewood, but the profit was very small. A few days ago, a friend, Shi Zhongjiu, bought a boatload of firewood from him, worth more than fifty yuan. Unexpectedly, after the firewood was loaded, the money was taken away to pay for the land. As a result, Qian Shuangfu had no way to make a living. He bought one yuan's worth of raw opium and swallowed it with wine. Soon after, the poison took effect. His wife rushed him to Guangji Hospital for treatment, but because he had taken a large amount of poison, his life was in danger.

Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway Adds Special Train for Tide Watching 120

The Qiantang River tide, every Mid-Autumn Festival, is surging and magnificent, a spectacular sight. Tens of thousands of Chinese and foreigners come to Zhejiang to watch the tide every year. The Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway has added a special train for tide watching. Because the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway has long been directly open to traffic, Shanghai and Haining are the only places on the Shanghai-Lai-Hangzhou route, tide watchers will inevitably change to the highway. In view of this, the Provincial Highway Bureau has decided to add a special Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway train for tide watching from the 29th of this month to facilitate tide watchers, starting from Minhang and ending at the Haining Bapu tide-watching destination. Two classes will run up and down the highway on the 8th, and Wang Shaoyi and Zhong Jihui have been assigned to be responsible for the preparation and reception matters. A number of tide-watching stands have been built in Haining, each of which can accommodate more than 500 people. Fearing that there will not be enough passenger cars at that time, travelers are specifically notified that they can make reservations in advance to avoid disappointment.

Siyang Radio Daily Reporter Assassinated 121

Mr. Qiao Cuili, a reporter for the Radio Daily in this county, went out on the afternoon of the 24th of last month and has not been heard from since. It was not until the 30th of last month that his family and colleagues [blank] were discovered outside the city at the old brick kiln at Wuditou with a bullet in his head and decaying muscles. Fortunately, there were clothes and other items that could be used for identification. The county government was requested to investigate, and it was confirmed that he had been shot to death before his death. County Magistrate Chen ordered the bereaved family to claim the body and bury it, and strictly ordered public security police to step up their efforts to arrest the perpetrators and bring them to justice.

Letter from the China International Famine Relief Commission 122

Dear Sirs, after reading the communication from Fenyi in your newspaper's report on its survey of Jiangxi, Anhui, Hunan and Hubei on August 22, it was stated that Magistrate Cheng Zhenxi of Qingjiang County said that the China International Famine Relief Commission had released a loan of 30,000 yuan, which had resulted in the farmers being harmed by unscrupulous local officials who extracted high interest rates and that the shortage of arable land this spring was because farmers had to sell their cattle to repay their debts, etc. After investigation, Qingjiang is not an agricultural relief county, but a cooperative county. The loan was handled by our association's office in Jiangxi, which only began operations in May of this year. The first repayment installment is not due until the end of this year. So, the so-called farmers selling cattle to repay their debts this spring is unclear. The paragraph in the above communication is obviously a misunderstanding of hearsay. As the matter concerns the future of cooperation, in addition to sending another letter to the Qingjiang County Magistrate for inquiry, we are sending this letter to request you to quickly correct the record in order to show the facts. Sincerely, the China International Famine Relief Commission, September 4.

Song Ziwen and Kong Xiangxi Returned to Shanghai Yesterday Aboard the Zhongshan Warship from Xunyang 123

Song did not receive guests due to a slight illness

Kong Attended the Mint Review Committee Meeting Immediately

Finance Minister Song Ziwen, after returning from overseas, proceeded to Nanjing and then to Jiangxi to attend the Lushan Conference, where he reported on the situation in Europe and America and discussed important issues such as diplomacy and domestic policy. With the conference now over, Song, accompanied by Central Bank Governor Kong Xiangxi and secretaries, traveled east from Jiujiang aboard the Zhongshan warship and arrived in Shanghai at 4:00 PM yesterday. Song suffered from diarrhea and returned to his residence to rest, declining to meet with guests. Detailed information is noted below.

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon 124

Mr. Song and Mr. Kong entered Nanjing and then went to Jiangxi to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and attend the Lushan Conference, a total of two days. Now that the meeting has ended, the two gentlemen, along with Song Zi'an, the Vice Minister of Finance and many others, boarded the Navy's Zhongshan warship at 9:00 AM the day before yesterday from Jiujiang to Shanghai. At 2:00 AM yesterday, they passed Nanjing without stopping and sailed straight to Shanghai. At 2:00 PM that afternoon, they entered the Wusong port.

Landed at Wusong 125

The Zhongshan warship carrying Mr. Song and Mr. Kong entered the port around 2:00 PM yesterday. At 2:30 PM, it docked opposite the Wusong Zhanghuabang Navy Pier. At that time, the outside world was unaware, so no one went to the pier to welcome them. Only Tang Hai'an, the Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, received a telegram from Song and specially dispatched the Customs' Jinghan small steamer to greet them. At the same time, Tang himself also took a car with the guards from the Kong and Song residences, in several cars, to the area to welcome them. After the ship docked, Tang took the Jinghan steamer to greet Kong, Song and others. At 3:10 PM, they disembarked from the naval pier and took several cars, arriving at the Song residence to rest at 4:05 PM. Mr. Kong went to the Central Bank on the Bund after arriving in Shanghai, delayed for a short time, and then returned to his residence.

Declined to Meet Guests 126

Those who arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon on the Zhongshan warship with Mr. Song and Mr. Kong included Song Zi'an, Mr. Song's brother, Zou Lin, the Permanent Vice Minister of Finance, Li Diaosheng, the Political Vice Minister, and secretaries Huang Chundao, Chen Fengyi, Chen Kangqi, and Qin Fen, a councilor, totaling seven people. Mr. Song did not stay long at the Lushan Conference, and came to Shanghai after the meeting. It was said that he was unwell. According to Secretary Huang Chundao, Mr. Song had diarrhea after arriving in Shanghai and therefore did not receive guests. Even Tang Hai'an, the Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, went to visit him after 4:00 PM.

Attended Review Meeting 127

Central Bank Governor Kong Xiangxi went to the Central Bank to attend to official business after arriving in Shanghai yesterday. He stayed for about ten minutes, then returned to his residence to rest and had some refreshments on the way. At 4:30 PM, he returned to the Central Bank to attend the Review Committee Meeting of the Central Mint. After the meeting adjourned at 5:30 PM, Mr. Kong went to the office to review accumulated documents until 7:30 PM before returning to his residence to rest.

Chinese and Foreign Relief Society Urgently Relieves Chuansha 139

The local Chinese and Foreign Relief Society, considering the ravages of the typhoon disaster in Chuansha, combined with the force of the waves, especially in Hengsha, Yuansha, and other places, which are islands formed by silt in the sea and often suffer disasters during major tides, found that on September 2nd, a sudden hurricane arose, with raging waves surging like mountains, causing the embankment to collapse completely, the entire island to be submerged, and the houses to drift away, with almost no survivors. People and livestock were drowned, and the number could not be counted. This catastrophe was an unprecedented disaster. There were 2,000 affected households and nearly 10,000 victims. Now that the storm has passed, the water has not completely receded. The victims are gathered at the embankment, without shelter or stored food, crying out in hunger and cold, calling for relatives and searching for companions, their tragic state of displacement reaching the sky. In addition, the decaying bodies of people and animals have not been completely buried, and the foul odor is breeding strange diseases. If they are not urgently relieved, there will be no survivors. Such a disaster is almost inhuman. Encountering such tragedy, they are still compatriots. Therefore, the society, in conjunction with the Jisheng Society, immediately raised several thousand yuan in foreign currency and rushed to Chuansha for emergency relief. However, with over ten thousand victims, it is inevitable that it will be like a drop in the bucket. It is hoped that all sectors will hear of this extraordinary disaster and provide assistance.

Reactions to the British Merchant's Tungsten Ore Monopoly 140

The Ministry of Industry entered into a tungsten ore export monopoly contract with the British firm Arnhold & Co. in June of this year. The standard tungsten ore was delivered on board ships at the Shanghai and Guangdong ports at only 500 yuan per ton. The tungsten miners in southern Jiangxi, working hard and not even having enough to eat, said that with the establishment of the monopoly bureau, their lives would be cut short. They petitioned for the cancellation of the original contract. The Hunan Mining Association also telegraphed the Ministry of Industry to cancel the monopoly contract and seek other appropriate relief measures.

Over five hundred people, including representatives from various sectors and reporters from newspapers, attended, making it a grand occasion. Welcoming Conference by Various Organizations (Photo Taken by Qichang Photography Studio) 144

After the meeting opened as scheduled, Chairman Tong Hangbai delivered a welcoming speech, stating that the Municipal Party Headquarters convened this meeting to welcome Comrade Sun, and its main significance lies in several points: (1) At present, China's political, economic, and social aspects all have many urgent problems to be solved. However, the issue of national survival is the foundation of all problems. In the past, China never paid attention to national defense and air defense, so it was breached and defenseless, allowing others to control it. Recently, the four northeastern provinces have been occupied by violence, this city has also been almost completely destroyed, and the nine small islands in the South China Sea have been plundered by France, entering and exiting as if in an uninhabited place. If the nation cannot survive, what other problems can be discussed? Therefore, if we want to solve the fundamental problem of national survival, we must concentrate our strength and strengthen national defense. Modern national defense is centered on air defense, so the manufacturing of aircraft and piloting talent should be widely cultivated and can no longer be purchased from foreign countries or recruited from other places. It is very obvious that Comrade Sun was able to fly an airplane across the Eurasian continent at a time when the whole country feels that talent is difficult to find, creating the only new record in China's aviation field, attracting the attention of the Chinese people to the aviation industry and jointly promoting its development. This is the point most worthy of our welcome. (2) China's science is backward and its culture is immature, so everything is inferior to others. In the past, the Generalissimo also

Mr. Sun Hosts the Press (Photo Taken by Qichang Photography Studio) 145

He once instructed us, "What we should learn from foreign countries is science, not politics. However, if we want to learn foreign science today, we must do so with the spirit of catching up head-on, so that we will not fall behind again." The youth in the country all know this principle, so over the years, the number of students going abroad to study has been no less than tens of millions. However, once they return to China after completing their studies, they cannot use what they have learned for its intended purpose. Since learning and application are contradictory, what they have learned is equivalent to not having learned it. There are many difficult reasons, but the weakness of their own will and the pursuit of immediate benefits are also among the reasons. Now, what Comrade Sun has learned in Europe is science, not politics. After completing his studies and returning to the country, he did not take a ship or train, but instead flew the airplane he had learned to fly, further expanding the use of what he had learned. Therefore, he has the grand undertaking of flying throughout the country to promote aviation. This point of "applying what has been learned" is enough to correct the bad habit of learning and application not matching, and this honor of flying back to the country can further encourage the rising youth to know that in addition to eating, taking an official position, there are also careers that can increase their status and develop their honor, so that they will not become bored and frustrated without a way out.

Reporting on the Experience 146

Then, Mr. Sun Tonggang reported on his experience, stating, "In 1928, I was sent to Germany by the central government to study aviation. After arriving in Germany from Shanghai, I studied German for half a year and then entered the Junkers and Siemens aircraft factories to work. Later, I entered a primary aviation school and gradually moved up to university. At university, I had a good grasp of piloting skills, so I bought today's airplane for practice. Since the September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident, I have been deeply stimulated and have worked even harder, knowing that in today's international situation, without a strong air force, it is impossible to enter the ranks of the strong. Among China's 400 million compatriots, no foreigner has ever known that there are Chinese aviators. Considering this, I had the long-distance return journey to the country. The tail of the plane was painted with the Party and national emblem, which suffered many setbacks. Later, after repeated negotiations with the German government, permission was finally obtained. My classmate, Mr. Li, saw my enthusiasm and wrote the Generalissimo's instruction 'Saving the country through aviation' on the plane, which made it even more noticeable. Since taking off from Germany on June 26th of this year until arriving in Guangdong, the most painful and difficult things in the process were, first, there was no equipment for weather testing along the way; second, there was a lot of rain in June, July, and August in the area. I was concerned that the airplane, which was made of very small pieces of wood glued together, would have pieces falling off once it rained; third, I had to fly at least eight hours a day, and sometimes eleven hours. After stopping, I had to add fuel, water, and repair parts, so I only had five hours of sleep each day, which made me feel very tired. Fourth, money could not be exchanged in various places. Every time I arrived at a place, I had to go to the bank to withdraw money. But although I felt all kinds of difficulties, I was eventually overwhelmed by the enthusiasm for saving the country through aviation and resolutely set off. At that time, I passed through the Balkans from Germany, through the desert areas around the Mediterranean Sea, where the flying sand was as high as 2,000 meters. When the wind rose, all directions were vast and dangerous, which was the most dangerous part of the flight. After passing through Arabia, Persia, Siam, Annam, India, and other places, I was isolated due to language barriers or detained by military authorities, which taught me a lot. But in the end, in a difficult environment, I was fortunate to have the spirit of the Generalissimo in heaven, and I was able to return to my motherland. This is a fortunate event." Then, Wang Zuwen reported (omitted).

Guest Speeches 147

Afterwards, Lin Wojiang gave an impassioned speech, saying, "Mr. Sun's return to the country from Europe, its danger and hardship, has been heard from Mr. Sun. Fortunately, Mr. Sun worked hard and advanced before returning safely to the motherland. This deserves our 120 points of joy. Tomorrow (the 9th), a naming ceremony for five aircraft will be held in this city. In addition to welcoming the aircraft, we also want to welcome aviation talents, because Mr. Sun will also go to the aircraft field tomorrow, and I will also keep Mr. Sun in Shanghai for a few more days to awaken the attention of people in this city to aviation. In the 20th century, a country without an air force can be said to be unadapted to the environment. A country that is not adapted to the environment, if it wants to survive in the world, its future is dangerous, to say the least. Aviation is extremely important to military affairs, that is, to transportation, and it also occupies a major application position. We hope that the nation will survive in the world, and aviation must be developed. Please pay special attention to it." After the speech, slogans were shouted and the meeting was adjourned.

Flying Around the City 148

Around 3 o'clock in the afternoon, Sun Tonggang, Wang Zuwen, and Lin Wojiang, the secretary-general of the Aviation Association, went to Hongqiao Airport in the same car. At 3:30, they boarded the aviation aircraft saving the nation and flew around the city in the urban area for a week and distributed propaganda. Then, they flew north to Jiangwan and Wusong, overlooking the ruins of the January 28th War Zone. At 4:30, they returned to Hongqiao, circled the field several times, and landed safely. After getting off the plane, Mr. Sun told a Central News Agency reporter that this trip was only one hour. The flight around Wusong was very low, from fifty meters to thirty, twenty, meters, and even skimmed the ground. Therefore, the destroyed fort was very clear to observe. When the reporter asked if he had any thoughts, he replied that he was deeply touched and could not express it in a few words.
