Around 10 o'clock, the hosts and guests happily dispersed.

Sichuan Organizations Report on the Reality of the Red Disaster in Sichuan 149

Sichuan Fellow Townsmen and Petition Group Yesterday Hosted the Press

The Committee for Relieving the Red Disaster in Western Sichuan of the Sichuan Sojourners Association in Shanghai and the Sichuan Northwestern Red Disaster Petition Group hosted the local press at 3:00 PM yesterday on the ninth floor of the YMCA at the Eight Immortals Bridge, reporting on the situation of the Red bandits harming Sichuan. Over twenty newspaper reporters attended. The various details are recorded below.

Chairman's Report 150

First, Chairman Li Fan briefly gave a welcoming speech. Then, Qiu Zhizhong reported on the significance of hosting the reporters, stating that the Red bandits in Sichuan occupied over 3,000 districts in more than ten places in northern Sichuan, including Tongjiang, Nanjiang, Bazhong, and Guangyuan. The number of people fleeing from these ten-plus counties to the east and west of Sichuan has reached over two million. For details, please ask the representatives of the group to report. I will not elaborate. However, after this serious incident, the telegram will detail the requests to the Executive Yuan of the government and the Disaster Relief Association, requesting them to quickly allocate large sums of money for emergency relief. Letters have also been sent to various charitable organizations and philanthropists in this city. In the two weeks since then, in addition to a batch of documents from the Disaster Relief Association, the government has not yet replied. We feel that the Red Disaster in Sichuan is no less than the floods. If the two million-plus victims are not rescued, those who dare to take risks out of hunger and cold are not a few. If the bandits fully absorb these two million-plus victims, the bandit trouble will expand even more. According to the report of the Military Affairs Commission, there are no more than 300,000 Red bandits. However, the government is spending tens of millions of troops, spending several years of effort, and spending hundreds of millions of money, and has not yet completely cleared them. If the refugees in the Red areas of northern Sichuan are not rescued, and seven times more are added to the Red Army's power, the future of the nation and the nation can be imagined. Moreover, when Chongqing, the capital of our province, suffered from the floods of the Yangtze River in the year of the Republic of China, Shanghai assisted, raising a total of 40,000 yuan for assistance. It can be imagined that the hearts of the benevolent have no distinction. Now, in addition to seeking help from the government based on the above-mentioned report, we also plan to invite fellow countrymen from Beijing and Shanghai, invite charitable organizations and philanthropists in this city, and beg for great compassion to help those victims, and to report on the needs of the press, for the mouthpieces of the people and the teachers of society. Please call on the world to ask for orders for more than two million refugees, so that they will not be forced to become bandits. Not only will our Association be grateful, but the rebirth of the victims will also be grateful in the future. Secondly, Liu Zizhong, the representative of the Petition Group, reported in detail on the Red Disaster and the victims' eager desire for rescue. His report on the process of the Red bandits harming Sichuan and the displacement of the victims is as follows:

The Course of the Red Disaster 151

It was found that the Xu and Kuang divisions had already been defeated by the central government's pursuit last winter, and only 7,000 or 8,000 bandits remained, entrenched in the border of Sichuan and Shaanxi. They were very short of bullets and had no fighting ability. By chance, the Sichuan army was in a civil war, and Liu Wenhui and Tian Leiyao were fighting in the province, resulting in an empty rear. Tongnanba, located on the border between Sichuan and Shaanxi, was taken advantage of by the Communist bandits and fell into the hands of the bandits. At this time, the troops stationed in Tongnanba and Baoning were from the third division of Luo Bochang. Luo was a soldier from the ranks, and he was extremely arrogant and domineering. He did everything he could to oppress the people. Before the Red bandits fell into Tongnanba last winter, he had levied more than 700,000 alcohol taxes in three months, all of which went into his private pockets. When the Red bandits came, he did not resist at all and abandoned the city and fled. This is why the Red bandits successively captured three counties. After the Red bandits captured the three counties of Tongnanba, they looted them extensively, and all the original social order was destroyed. As a result, more than 100,000 people were displaced. This was the first fall. On the social side, there was considerable strength to provide relief to these displaced refugees. In May of this year, Liu Wenhui, the chairman of Sichuan Province, attacked the Deng army, ignoring the national crisis. Tian and Deng depended on each other, and they withdrew the troops to assist Deng. The Xu and Kuang bandits, who had already been defeated, took the opportunity to counterattack and recapture the three counties of Tongnanba. Recently, a letter from Sichuan stated that the strength of the Red bandits had increased three or four times, and the area they occupied was also larger than before. In counties such as Yilong and Cangxi, more than two-thirds of the villages outside the county area were occupied by the Communist bandits. Moreover, it is close to the autumn harvest, and the Communist bandits are looting everywhere, and they are stockpiling the looted food in Cangba Changchi Enyang River, etc., with a long-term plan. On the one hand, the Soviet People's Bank was reorganized in Tongjiang, and the Sichuan-Shaanxi Provincial Soviet Government was established in Bazhong, showing that the Communist bandits were really Red in both Sichuan and Shaanxi.

Victims Displaced 152

It was found that Tongnanba was first trapped, and it was the end of the old lunar calendar, and the people's homes still had a little storage, so Dada could barely escape. Moreover, at that time, the area occupied by the Communist bandits was small, and the impact was not great, so the number of displaced people was only 100,000. The second trapping, the slaughter of the Communist bandits was even more tragic than before. The people were afraid of being killed and fled their homes one after another. The people of the three counties of Tongnanba fled to Guqing, Jianzhong, Yilong, Nanbu, Yingshan, Daxian, Quxian, and Xuanhan. In the northwest counties of Wen, there were no places without victims. The tragic displacement was beyond words. At this time, the victims in various places are mostly 100 people living in one place, steamed by heat, suffering from hunger and disease, and those who died from infectious diseases cannot be counted, and even those who died in the whole family can be described as the most tragic things in the world.

Purpose of the Petition 153

The people of the northwestern counties of Sichuan are now in a dire situation. Those who have already fallen into the counties are suffering unspeakable pain, while those who have not fallen into the counties are raising a class of corrupt local ruffians, who are mostly willing to be the claws of warlords, causing the people to have no way out and no way to live. The reason for this is that the Red bandits entrenched on the border between northern Sichuan must first be wiped out. Therefore, (1) Please clear the Red bandits of the central government, and (2) Please relieve the victims of the central government.

The 20,000-Mile Long-Distance Propaganda Experience of the National Disaster Propaganda Group of the United States 155

Through Eleven Provinces Including Jiangsu, Hubei, Hunan, Hebei, Shanxi, Chahar, and Suiyuan

Brought Back a Large Number of Items to be Exhibited in Beijing and Shanghai

And Plans for a Second Long-Distance National Disaster Propaganda

The National Disaster Propaganda Group of Students from Shanghai Art College, with the support of the central government, set off from Beijing in January of this year, and spent seven months in the Yangtze River, North China, and the Mongolian border, carrying out national disaster propaganda, traveling 20,000 miles. After the first phase of propaganda work was completed, it returned to Shanghai on the 5th of this month. A reporter from Shanghai Social News Agency specially visited Mr. Shen Yiqian, the head of the group, yesterday to discuss the propaganda experience and future plans as follows:

Origin of Departure 156

Mr. Shen said that since the loss of Shenyang on September 18, he recognized that this was the beginning of the country's peril. Therefore, he was determined to perish in the Northeast

The Buddhist Monk of Inner Mongolia Resides at Wudang Tai, Only Fifteen Years Old, Possessing Exceptional Intelligence 157

Advocating the principle of "saving China by saving the Northeast, which is saving ourselves," he gathered seven like-minded comrades to form a National Crisis Propaganda Group. Initially, they engaged in propaganda in Shanghai, creating propaganda posters and sending them to Canada, the Philippines, the South Seas Islands, the the United States, and other places to attract global attention. During the January 28th Shanghai Incident, the group engaged in frontline propaganda. After the war, feeling the lack of protection in the airspace, they also promoted national salvation through aviation on behalf of the China Aviation Association. Since the loss of Yuguan and the instability of North China, lamenting the imminent fall of the nation, they immediately packed up a few painting tools and resolutely set out for various provinces to conduct long-distance propaganda. On one hand, they exposed the enemy's conspiracies and atrocities, and on the other hand, they inspired the people to raise funds for self-salvation in order to rescue the endangered China.

The Propaganda Journey 158

Mr. Shen then stated, "Our group departed from Shanghai at the end of January this year for Beijing, a total of seven people. After arriving in Beijing, we immediately held a National Crisis Painting Exhibition at the Confucius Temple. More than 50,000 people visited, including central figures such as Chairman Lin. Subsequently, with the support of the central government, we traveled upstream along the Yangtze River in mid-February, stopping at Hankou. After about two weeks of propaganda, we crossed the river to Wuchang, where we held a National Crisis Painting Exhibition at the Provincial Public Education Hall, adding lantern slides and posting front-line pictorials. At the same time, at the request of various circles in Wuhan, we specially painted multiple "Aviation Saves the Nation" pictures for widespread promotion, creating a very tense atmosphere. In early March, we transferred to Changsha. The number of people who received our group's propaganda was over 100,000, and the public spirit was high, leaving the best impression. At that time, there were five people traveling together. Due to academic commitments, they returned to Shanghai. However, considering the deepening war in North China, I resolutely went north on April 7 to participate in the war zone propaganda. I also held a National Crisis Painting Exhibition in the Central Park of Beiping, where there were direct conflicts with the Japanese. The public spirit of my hometown was greatly inspired. After the Tanggu Truce was signed, I immediately...

Journeyed Alone Beyond the Great Wall 159

I conducted propaganda in the Chahar area and was once detained by troops under Feng Yuxiang's command. At the end of May, I left Zhangjiakou and traveled on foot to Suiyuan and Liaoning, holding a National Exhibition at the Mongolian Temple in Jinlitu Tai. I also distributed a large number of promotional booklets and color pictorials, all with explanations in Mongolian, to approach the Mongolian people. Old and young alike came to visit, and they were deeply moved. At the end of June, I went to Baotou to focus on Mongolian and Hui propaganda. Then I went to Ulanqab League in northern Suiyuan to visit the life of the Mongolian people. Alone in the northern wilderness, I was surrounded by bandits in the mountains about a hundred miles from Baotou and was almost killed, barely escaping with my life. The second time, I repacked my belongings in Baotou and once again went to Inner Mongolia, heading to Wudang Tai, the largest and most famous temple inside and outside Yinshan Mountain, to conduct interviews. The executive officers treated me as a distinguished guest and presented me with a Mongolian dog. After four days of collecting information, I conducted a concrete investigation of Mongolian education, folk life, and nomadic conditions, and took more than a hundred photographs and dozens of sketches. At the end of July, I returned to Baotou and collected more than a hundred kinds of woolen textiles from the Northwest. Then I took the Beiping-Pukou Railway back to Beijing to make a report to the central government. On the fifth of this month, I rushed back to Shanghai. In total, this trip lasted seven months, passing through eleven provinces, with a journey of about 20,000 li."

Future Plans 160

Future plans: (1) Preparing for a North China Sketch Exhibition, with locations set in Nanjing and Shanghai. It is currently in preparation. (2) Establishing a Northwest Native Products Purchasing and Sales Office. (3) Planning a second long-distance propaganda trip, determined to traverse about fifteen provinces in the northwest, southwest, and southeast, a journey of 35,000 li. The purposes are: 1. Anti-Japanese national salvation propaganda. 2. Exchanging feelings among various ethnic groups. 3. Uniting the national spirit. 4. Investigating the border situation. 5. Compiling the results into a systematic book for the reference of the people of the country.

Mongolian Yurt 161

Departing for Beijing Today 162

Finally, Mr. Shen told the reporter that he will lead the group members, carrying a large number of collected materials and various sketches and photos, to Beijing by express train this afternoon. Last week, we held a North China Sketch Exhibition at the Confucius Temple and prepared the procedures for the group's second long-distance propaganda work. We will return to Shanghai in about two weeks. After returning to Shanghai, we will hold a sketch exhibition in this city, and at the latest around Double Tenth Day, we will start our second long-distance propaganda trip to the north.

A Strange Iron Box Suddenly Appears in West Yaojia Lane 163

A Huge Hole Chiseled in the Bottom of the Box

No One Claims It

Related to the China Land Reclamation Bank's Missing Money Case: The China Land Reclamation Bank recently shipped 70,000 yuan of silver dollars from its Ningbo branch to Shanghai, entrusting it to Wei Yuming, a steward on the New Ning-Shao steamer of the Ning-Shao Company. Unexpectedly, upon arrival in Shanghai, a huge hole was suddenly discovered in the bottom of the iron box containing the money, and the 70,000 yuan of silver dollars inside had been stolen, leaving only 210 yuan. At the time, Tang, who shared the room and was on the run, was suspected of being heavily involved. The bank sent letters to the British and French concessions and the Water Police Bureau requesting his arrest, and formally posted a reward notice. However, as of this morning, the escaped Tang and the lost 69,790 yuan of silver dollars have not been recovered. However, around 7 p.m. the night before, an ownerless iron box was suddenly discovered on the roadside at the entrance of West Yaojia Lane in the city. The box was about two feet long, more than a foot wide, and the height and style were the same as the iron boxes used exclusively by banks to transport money. The strangest thing was that the bottom of this box, like the bottom of the iron box containing the missing money from the China Land Reclamation Bank, had a huge hole chiseled by thieves using iron tools. However, the box was empty. It was discovered by police officer Han Tinghu in charge of that area. After waiting for a long time, the owner still did not come to claim it. Therefore, the box was taken to the Second Precinct of the First District, where Director Liu inspected it. Because the box arrived so strangely, it was deemed to be related to the China Land Reclamation Bank's missing money case. At around noon yesterday, he ordered his subordinates to prepare a document and send the box to the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau for filing. At the same time, a senior police officer was dispatched to investigate the origin of the box.

Customs Seizes a Huge Smuggling Case of Military Supplies 164

A Total of Thirty-Nine Latest Model Automatic Pistols

Thirty-Six Magazine Clips and Four Thousand Bullets

According to the Shanghai Times, it has been learned that customs officials cracked a major case of smuggling a large amount of military supplies on Wednesday night and arrested several suspects. The military supplies included a total of thirty-nine pistols, mostly the latest model automatic pistols, thirty-six magazine clips, and four thousand bullets. They were found on the Glenogle, a ship of the Chata Company that sailed from the United Kingdom and various ports in Europe. When the ship arrived at the port at 5 p.m. on Wednesday afternoon, customs officers boarded the ship for inspection as usual. They then found the military supplies in the drawers of an empty cabin occupied by the engineer. At that time, it was suspected that a Chinese servant in the engine room was involved in the smuggling. Therefore, they paid close attention that night and arrested several suspected Chinese in the early morning. The investigation is still ongoing. According to reports, it is common for customs to seize smuggled military supplies, but usually only three or four items. Such a large-scale smuggling case is rare.

Japanese Vice-Consul Requests the Extradition of Chinese National Jin Shuishan 165

Why is Japan Concerned About the Murder of an American Citizen by a Chinese National?

Jin Shuishan, a Korean who has become a Chinese national, is now 23 years old. He had previously studied at a certain military academy. His ancestors were originally Korean, but his father and others had become Chinese citizens since childhood. Therefore, Shuishan had long become a pure Chinese. During the January 28th Incident, Jin joined a certain artillery battalion and killed countless enemies, making many meritorious achievements. Therefore, he was hated by the enemy to the bone. They repeatedly sent people to secretly investigate and arrest him, and devised plans to harm him. However, because Jin was extremely vigilant on weekdays, they could not find an opportunity to strike. After the Shanghai War ended and the agreement was signed, Jin was re-hired by the Central Artillery School as a training officer, working hard in teaching and sparing no effort. Recently, due to important matters, he planned to go to Guangdong. Therefore, he came to Shanghai a few days ago and boarded the Yi Sun steamer to set off. However, because the ship had not reached the departure date, it had not yet set anchor as of yesterday, so it was still berthed next to the Sixteenth Pier of the South City. Unexpectedly, Jin's whereabouts were suddenly known by treacherous people, who secretly reported to the Japanese Consulate, falsely accusing him of assassinating Liu Yinfa, a Korean who had become an American citizen. At around 2 p.m. yesterday afternoon, Vice-Consul Saeki Tasuke reported to the Third Precinct of the Fifth District of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau, requesting assistance in the arrest. The Director of the precinct, Wen Yishan, knowing that the Huangpu River was under the jurisdiction of the Water Patrol Team and that the precinct lacked personnel proficient in Japanese, sent Li Jiachi, a clerk from the First Precinct of the Fifth District, to accompany the Japanese Vice-Consul to the South City Water Patrol Headquarters. Commander Zhu dispatched several senior police officers to board a patrol boat and rush to the surface of the Huangpu River at the Sixteenth Pier. They boarded the Yi Sun steamer and arrested Jin Shuishan, bringing him back to the team. After a brief interrogation by Commander Zhu, he was handed over to Clerk Li and brought back to the Third Precinct of the Fifth District. At that time, the Japanese Vice-Consul immediately requested permission to extradite Jin back to the consulate for interrogation. However, Director Wen did not approve the extradition because the Japanese Consulate claimed that Jin was the murderer who assassinated Liu Yinfa, but did not provide any substantial evidence. He will send personnel to conduct a detailed investigation and then submit a report to Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau Chief Wen Hongen for approval before proceeding.

A Woman is Robbed and Shot to Death 166

Shot in the Chest, She Dies on the Spot

Yang Bingfa, a native of Ningbo, 60 years old, lived at No. 21 Yong'an Lane, Zhoushan Road, Zhoujiazui Road. The bullet did not penetrate, and she collapsed to the ground, bleeding profusely. She died on the spot. Seeing the tragedy, the thieves fled. Rabid Dog Kills Person in Gaochang Temple, Health Bureau Announces Emergency Treatment Methods 168

A rabid dog has been found in the Zhuhu Road area of Gaochang Temple, and several children have been bitten. One 16-year-old boy has died of poisoning. The rabid dog has also been killed by people. However, there are many stray dogs in the area, and there are still many dogs that appear to be rabid. Nearby citizens are afraid to approach. The Shanghai Tongshan Xizi Association in the area specially petitioned the Municipal Health Bureau for relief. After receiving the report, the bureau immediately sent personnel to investigate. Yesterday, Dr. Zhang Bingrui of the Health Education Division of the bureau published methods for preventing rabid dog bites to the Shen Shi News reporter. According to Dr. Zhang, the toxicity of rabid dog bites usually develops within 14 to 40 days. Therefore, treatment should be sought quickly during this period. Once the toxicity has developed, there is little hope of recovery. There are two emergency treatment methods: (1) Treatment of the wound: Strong nitric acid can be used to cauterize the wound, or fire can be used for cauterization. (2) Pasteur rabies treatment: you can go to a hospital, or the Public Works Bureau and the Health Bureau, etc., to inject a special vaccine to resist the rabies virus. The fundamental method is to control rabid dogs. The Health Bureau is actively working on this, and it is hoped that citizens will also pay attention.

Two Uncles and Nephews Conspire to Deceive 150 People 170

Established the Nanyang Langge Timber Firm Worker Introduction Agency

Recruited Workers Everywhere, Each Person Had to Pay a Huge Deposit

丨Thirty-Six People Appeared in Court Yesterday to Testify丨

Zhou Lichun, a native of Yangzhou, 46 years old, was a doctor. Recently, due to the lack of patients, his nephew Zhou Jincai, who had previously worked at the American Langge Foreign Firm at No. 1 Huangpu Road, was sent to the Langge Timber Firm in Pulo Ro, Nanyang Islands. After resigning this spring, he lived idly with his uncle Zhou Lichun at No. 18 Songmao Lane, Songpan Road, Yangshupu. The two uncles and nephews recently came up with a fraudulent scheme, falsely claiming that the branch of the foreign firm, the Nanyang Langge Timber Firm, wanted to hire a large number of workers who could earn a monthly salary of 50 or 60 yuan. They established an introduction agency at their residence, printed cards, with Zhou Jincai as the chief foreman, and invited several assistants to recruit workers everywhere, each person having to pay a deposit of 20 or 30 yuan. From January to this month, 150 people were deceived. On the 31st of last month, the case was solved by Chinese Detective Liu Wenzao and Detectives Guo Jingbang and No. 2568 of the Yangshupu Police Station. Zhou Lichun, Zhou Jincai, and their accomplices Zhou Jinbao, Fei Zhaofeng, Xu Hechun, Wei Fu, Jin Yushan, Lv Zhenmao, Wang Dewu, Du Honglong, Zhou Lisen, and other eleven people were arrested one after another, along with recruitment cards, name books, fake seals, and a large bundle of letters from the victims asking when they would depart. They were taken to the police station the next morning and sent to the simple court of the First Special District for investigation. Now that the case should be heard by the local court, the police station sent it to the Criminal Third Court yesterday morning. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin first described the case, saying that at around 10 a.m. this morning, twenty-six victims were making a fuss at the door of the introduction agency established by the two Zhous. Police officers asked what was the matter. They claimed that they had been recruited by the introduction agency to work at the Nanyang Langge Timber Firm, and had paid the deposit for many months, but the agency had not fulfilled its promise to send them to work. The detectives knew it was a fraudulent organization and arrested the defendants. During the subsequent investigation, it was found that Zhou Lichun was in charge of the accounting, Zhou Jincai was responsible for going out to recruit workers and collect money, and the others were assistants. According to Zhou Jincai, in May of this year, he met a Turkish man named Iman Mateng, who was an employee of the Langge Foreign Firm. He asked him to recruit workers to go to Nanyang to work and to provide a guarantee letter. Later, he entrusted a Westerner named Luo Sibo, who was an inspector at the Nanyang Langge Timber Firm, to write a letter of introduction. The letter was handed to him at the entrance of the Langge Foreign Firm at No. 1 Huangpu Road, and he recruited workers on his behalf. The first deposit was 120 yuan, and the second time it was 270 yuan. All were paid to Iman at the entrance of the foreign firm. It was found that Iman had previously worked in the Langge warehouse on Huade Road. On April 2 of this year, he embezzled 1,000 yuan and fled without a trace. The police arrested him, but have not yet caught him. Iman has a brother who works at the British American Tobacco Company, and his girlfriend lives at No. 937 North Sichuan Road. His boyfriend is named Lai Baier and lives at No. 72 on the same road. The police have repeatedly inquired at these three locations, but all said they have not seen Iman in Shanghai recently. Therefore, Zhou Jincai's confession is also unreliable. Zhou Lichun claimed that the matter was entirely done by his nephew Jincai and that he did not know the details. The others were evasive. It was found that the total amount of fraud was about 700 yuan. The total number of workers recruited was 250, and it has been found that 150 people were deceived. Today, thirty-six victims appeared in court, and the others could not be summoned. The case is requested to be postponed, and all the evidence will be presented for inspection. Subsequently, victims Lu Qingming, He Wenli, and others testified to the fraud. Judge Liu Yugui ordered the defendants to be remanded and adjourned the hearing.

The Yangtze River Navy Will Hold a Grand Review in Shanghai 174

To be held on the 15th outside Woosung

Another Demonstration of Militaristic Country's Power

After the Japanese Navy held grand maneuvers, its fleets stationed abroad also held grand reviews. The First Foreign Squadron stationed in the Yangtze River, since the Japanese Naval Ministry added the Third Fleet to Shanghai, in addition to the 24th and 27th Destroyer Squadrons and the cruiser Tenryu stationed in Shanghai, the 14 warships of the First Foreign Squadron in the Yangtze River, managed by Rear Admiral Sakamoto, are also under the command of Vice Admiral Minei, commander of the Second Fleet stationed in Shanghai. The Japanese Naval Ministry has already sent a report to Shanghai stating that the Third Fleet's warships will hold a grand exercise outside Woosung on the 15th of this month. In addition to all the ships stationed in Shanghai participating in the gathering, the warships of the First Foreign Squadron stationed in various ports along the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River will also be ordered by Vice Admiral Minei to be transferred to Shanghai by Commander Sakamoto to join the exercise. According to statistics, the Japanese Navy in the Yangtze River and Shanghai, under the jurisdiction of the Third Fleet, has a total of 23 ships, plus 2,200 marines. There are also hundreds of military personnel. Among the marines, there are artillery teams, machine gun teams, tank teams, and newly formed hygiene teams, etc. A large number of military engineering teams transferred from Sasebo by the Naval Ministry last month are still actively working in the new military camp in Shanghai, building various special equipment for military purposes. In addition, since January 28th, seven or eight hundred police officers have been successively transferred from police departments across Japan to Shanghai to be trained in what is known as a "mobile police force" that is familiar with the situation in the Chinese interior, with a profound purpose.

The Continental News reported that in recent weeks, foreign military and diplomatic officials in this port seem to be showing signs of anxiety and uneasiness. According to a foreign consul in this port who told a reporter from the Continental News yesterday, this phenomenon is due to the completion of the huge military barracks built by the Japanese at the end of North Sichuan Road, which is about to hold a completion ceremony. The foreign consuls and officers whom the reporter met, although unwilling to reveal their names, all had a feeling that in the past ten months, the Japanese army has been working day and night to build a four-story huge barracks that is 525 feet long and 225 feet wide, and its importance is probably not just for stationing troops. Many foreign military leaders in this port call this military camp practically a fortress. The Japanese are obviously intending to make this militarily important location a well-equipped stronghold. According to Tokyo newspapers last week, more than 2,000 Japanese naval personnel have already moved into it. A reporter from a local newspaper witnessed a large number of munitions being transported into the camp on the 27th of last month, and armed sentries were tightly guarding all gates. In addition, Chinese and foreign officials in this port also learned from Tokyo newspapers that the Japanese Navy has chosen to hold maneuvers near Woosung on September 15th, and at the same time hold a grand completion ceremony for this military camp. Japanese warships stationed in Hankou, Wuhu, Changsha, and other places have been ordered by the Japanese Naval Ministry to go to Woosung for maneuvers, and it is also heard that several senior naval officers will come to Shanghai for inspection. Those concerned about this matter also pointed to the military hospital next to the military camp. It is said that the hospital has four stories, with a facade almost half the size of the entire camp. Japanese newspapers estimate that the cost of building the military camp and the hospital should be more than 2 million yen, which shows the depth of their intentions. Although the construction of this huge building only started ten months ago, it was able to be completed on schedule. According to foreign officers in Shanghai, the structure of the camp is almost entirely modeled after the infantry camp of the 3rd Division of the Tokyo Kiniki, so it can be completed quickly within this short period. The hospital and the military camp are built with steel and concrete, which can withstand fierce artillery fire. The top of the camp can be equipped with 5-inch guns, and firing will not damage the camp building, which is so strong. According to military experts, the windows of the North Sichuan Road camp are cleverly designed to place machine guns to fire in three directions. All doors in the camp are fitted with all-steel doors. The interior of the camp can accommodate 2,000 to 600 people for exercises. There is also a Chan temple for soldiers to worship. The camp also has small rooms for placing armored vehicles and tanks, and warehouses for storing large quantities of ammunition. It is said that electricity and water can be supplied from a certain place in Zhabei. The Japanese built this camp, and others paid little attention to it at first. After it was built, it was so large and strong that once a war breaks out, it can be used as a base regardless of whether it is for defense or offense. Therefore, it is not yet known whether various countries will protest or send more troops to Shanghai. However, according to foreign military experts, building a barracks resembling a fortress on Chinese soil violates the 1922 Washington Treaty. The treaty was signed by the United States, Belgium, Britain, France, Italy, Japan, the Netherlands, and other countries, stipulating that foreign troops should be withdrawn immediately unless permitted by the treaty. Japan also ratified this treaty. After the Washington Conference ended, Japan withdrew its troops from Hankou and Shandong in accordance with the treaty. The number of troops stationed by the old allied countries in the north was only as stipulated in the Boxer Protocol. Troops could not be sent ashore again except in extremely urgent circumstances. After foreign troops landed in Tianjin, Hankou, Shanghai, and other places in 1927, they were withdrawn soon after. Only Shanghai has not been completely withdrawn, but the foreign troops stationed there are only temporarily stationed. Therefore, their military camps are rented or built with wood. As soon as the Chinese government can fully protect foreign nationals, they can be completely withdrawn. Since last year, they have been withdrawing successively. Currently, the foreign troops stationed in Shanghai include 2,000 American troops, 2,100 British troops, 1,400 French troops, 2,000 Japanese troops, and 1,100 members of the International Settlement Volunteer Corps.

Silk Mill Workers Resumed Work Yesterday Morning, but Struck Again in the Afternoon Due to Misunderstanding 175

Sixteen Companies Including Yuanxing All Suspended Again

Factories in the Settlement Did Not Operate Yesterday Due to Machine Repairs

According to the Ta Kung She, female workers in silk mills in the Zhabei district went on strike due to opposition to the production quota system. After mediation by the Social Affairs Bureau, it was announced that work would resume. Unexpectedly, work resumed twice and then went on strike again, and the strike also spread to five factories in the Settlement, including Yuyuan. Yesterday morning, the silk mills in the Zhabei district started work as usual, and all the workers entered the factories. Unexpectedly, in the afternoon, the workers of Yuanxing Factory on Yutong Road in Zhabei went on strike again due to a misunderstanding, and all factories immediately stopped work. The situation is very complicated. It is hoped that work will resume fully this morning. The details are as follows:

Work Resumed Yesterday Morning 176

At 5:30 yesterday morning, the 21 silk mills on Changan Road, Yutong Road, Guangfu Road, and Xinzhabei Meiyuan Road in Zhabei, including Chuxin, Hongchun, and Yuanxing, started work as usual. All the female workers in the factories entered the factories one after another. The Silk Workers' Union of the Sixth District, fearing that changes would occur again, specially sent all the directors and supervisors, Yang Geng, Wu Suzhen, Yuan Yunlong, and Li Tonggai, etc., to persuade them separately. Dozens of police officers from the Police Brigade and the Public Security Bureaus of the Fourth and Second Districts were also dispatched to the factories to protect the workers. Hongchun Silk Factory on Guangfu Road planned to release the female workers because there were not enough workers. The union, fearing that it would cause another misunderstanding, immediately consulted with the factory and temporarily maintained the start of work, so the order was good and no incident occurred.

Trouble Started Again 177

Unexpectedly, at 1:00 p.m. after lunch, when work was about to start, a piece of paper for donating to the Taiping Gongjiao was posted at the gate of Yuanxing Silk Factory on Yutong Road, with donations ranging from two to three corners. Unexpectedly, the female workers of the factory mistakenly thought that the factory had announced the production quota system, and there was a lot of noise for a while, and they unanimously refused to enter the factory. They also went to various factories such as Wuxing Lun on Meiyuan Road to spread rumors, and the order became chaotic again. Therefore, the 15 silk mills on Changan Road, including Chuxin, Hongchun, Yuanxin, Xiexin, Hongsheng, Xiexing, Jiyu, Zhenxing Yuji, Baotaisunji, on Gonghe Road, Jiyuyingji, on Guangxu Road, Jiatai, on Hengfeng Road, Meifeng, and Yuanfeng, stopped work automatically, fearing that workers would come to cause trouble. Only the three factories on Changan Road, Maofeng, Fuxing, and Yuanli, continued to work as usual.

Situation in the Settlement 178

The five silk mills in the Settlement, including Taixin on Alabaster Road, Yuanhe, Jingwei, Xiangyuan on Gansu Road, and Yuyuan on Guoqing Road, were affected by the strike the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning, because Taixin and Xiangyuan Silk Factories needed to repair the engine and furnace, they did not start work yesterday. This morning, except for Taixin and Yuanhe Factories, the other three factories, Jingwei, Xiangyuan, and Yuyuan, decided to start work as usual. The workers of the three factories are also allowed to enter the factory and resume work.

Investigation of Work Resumption 179

After the workers of the 21 silk mills in the Xinzhabei and Zhabei districts experienced labor unrest, the other 12 factories, such as Beifengtai, Fuchang, Yutai, Gongda, Tiansheng, Hongyu, Yingji, Hengcang, Xinglun, and Yufeng, north of the railway, and the two factories, Yuantai and Ruilun, on Guangfu Road, started work as usual and were not affected. Yesterday morning, the three factories on Changan Road, Maofeng, Fuxing, and Yuanli, also resumed work. According to statistics, 17 factories in the Zhabei district have resumed work, while 16 factories are still suspended.

Party Department Thoroughly Investigates 180

The Municipal Party Department, according to the report of the Silk Workers' Union of the Sixth District, said that there were more changes in the 16 silk mills in the Xinzhabei and Zhabei districts. It was said that there must be bad elements agitating and deliberately playing tricks. Yesterday afternoon, the Municipal Party Department specially sent cadres of the Civil Affairs Section, Lu Yinchu and Fan Guoren, etc., to the Xinzhabei and Zhabei districts to thoroughly investigate the truth and decided to strictly investigate it. It also ordered the Silk Workers' Union of the Sixth District to be responsible for ordering all workers to resume work from this morning and not to cause further incidents.

The Federation of Commerce and Industry Recommends the Reason for Jointly Sharing Liabilities 181

Issue of Amending Article 681 of the Civil Code

The National Federation of Commerce and Industry previously requested the Legislative Yuan to amend Article 68 of the Civil Code. After receiving a reply from the Secretariat of the Legislative Yuan, which was approved and referred to the Civil Law Committee for reference, yesterday, it supplemented four reasons and contributed methods, again on behalf of the National Government Legislative Yuan. To the Legislative Yuan in Nanjing, greetings. We have found that Article 681 of the Civil Code on Debt, which states that when the partnership property is insufficient to pay off the partnership's debts, each partner shall bear joint and several liability, is difficult to implement in practice. The subordinate association reported to your esteemed Yuan on July of this year, requesting that it be amended. On August 6, your esteemed Yuan Secretariat sent a letter stating that the regulations of Article 681 of the Civil Code have an impact on the future of commerce and are indeed correct. We request that the article be amended to share partnership debts according to shares, in order to maintain the inherent habit of fairness. There is a power report, which was approved and referred to the Civil Law Committee of this hospital for reference, etc. In addition to the transfer, the corresponding letter is sent for reference. Now, the 81st proposal of the National Industry and Commerce Conference in 19 years is a suggestion from the Chongqing Chamber of Commerce in Sichuan that the joint and several liability for partnership business stipulated in the Civil Code has caused difficulties. We request that you formulate supplementary provisions and forward them to the Legislative Yuan for supplementary relief. Therefore, we know that the difficulty of this case has not only started today. However, when the Civil Code was promulgated at that time, the difficulties were few. Until today, the difficulties have gradually appeared and the disputes have increased. I am afraid that new partnership organizations will disappear because of this, and the old ones will also be afraid. How can we deal with partnership organizations that account for 78% of the commercial market in our country? This case concerns the prosperity and decline of the national business community, which is extremely important. The subordinate association is deeply worried about the future. There are still four requests for immediate amendments to your esteemed hospital: The first is that Article 677 of the Civil Code stipulates that the number of profit and loss distributions shall be determined according to the proportion of each partner's investment if it has not been agreed upon. This article has clearly stipulated that profits and losses shall be shared according to shares, while Article 681 of the same law stipulates that partnership debts shall be jointly and severally liable. The meanings before and after are also contradictory. This should be amended first. The law is nothing more than human donation, and human feelings are based on habit. Sharing partnership profits and losses equally is a fair habit in our country. Even if there are occasional leaks , we can only find ways to remedy them in other ways, or limit registration. If we deviate from it and become a law, then this law is outside of human feelings and will not be applicable and difficult to implement. This should be requested for amendment second. Considering the original intention of legislation at that time, it was originally afraid that cunning people would borrow money in the name of eliminating goods. Once they go bankrupt, no one will be responsible. Legislation is not inconsiderate, but its effect is the opposite. Those who are cunning will share the debt equally after bankruptcy. Although there is no money to pay back, they will inevitably be involved in lawsuits. Now they share the losses equally and are jointly and severally liable. Who would not want this benefit? In the future, the dishonest will regard the business community as a trap, and the cunning will regard partnerships as scams. This should be requested for amendment third. If everything is not balanced, there will be鳴. Rights and obligations must be absolutely equal to be called平. According to the provisions of Article 681 of the Civil Code, it is to enable partners to enjoy limited rights and fulfill unlimited obligations. Rights and obligations are unbalanced, and if they are not平, it will be difficult to implement and disputes will arise spontaneously. This should be requested for amendment fourth. Based on the above four points, it is reasonable to submit them again to your esteemed Yuan for inspection. We earnestly request that the text of Article 681 of the Civil Code be amended promptly. If the amendment is difficult, then or after the amendment, add a section that "However, if the partnership has been approved by the local competent authority for registration or registration, this limit shall not apply." At the same time, consult with the Executive Yuan and transfer the order to the Ministry of Industry to notify the shops organized by partnerships across the country to follow the procedure. A foolish idea, please adopt and implement it to benefit the business community. Sincerely, Chairman of the National Federation of Commerce and Industry, Lin Kanghou, Qiyin, September 8, 22nd year of the Republic of China.

Only the Amount of the Increased Assessment is Discounted by 20%

Overturned Nitric Acid Spills on the Ground, Rickshaw Puller Falls Victim 200

Female Passenger in the Rickshaw Also Injured in Her Left Foot

The Culprit Rickshaw Puller Flees Without a Trace

Yesterday morning at around 11:00 AM, on Xi Zang Road, a handcart (commonly known as a "tiger cart") carrying two jars of nitric acid was slowly approaching from the direction of Yun Nan Road. When it reached the front of the New Eastern Hotel, due to improper placement, one of the jars in the middle fell from the cart and shattered on the spot. The nitric acid spilled all over the ground, and the pungent smell of acid filled the air. Just as the rickshaw puller was about to clean up, a rickshaw sped around the corner and was about to run into the nitric acid. Upon seeing this, bystanders, fearing an accident, shouted for him to avoid it. However, it was too late. At the same time, the rickshaw puller became anxious and flustered, and without due care, he lost his footing and fell backward, landing completely in the nitric acid. The clothes he was wearing were instantly eroded, and his skin was also affected. A female passenger in the rickshaw luckily did not fall, and only her left foot stepped into the acid, so her injury was relatively minor. The rickshaw puller screamed for help in agony. Upon seeing this, the handcart puller abandoned his cart and fled. Fortunately, nearby police officers had already been alerted and rushed to the scene. They immediately telegraphed the Lao Zha Police Station to send a car to rush the rickshaw puller and the female passenger to Ren Ji Hospital for treatment. It is reported that the rickshaw puller's name is Xu Bao Shu, 33 years old, from Jiang Bei. He suffered injuries to his back and left foot. The female passenger's name is Yao Tang Shi, 40 years old, and she injured her left foot. As for the escaped handcart puller, the police are currently investigating.

Two Women Arrested in the Private Tutor Murder Case 201

Wenfa College Poorly Run by Outlying Districts 207

丨Closing Time Can Be Appropriately Extended丨

(Central 8th Nanjing Telegram) A person in charge of the Ministry of Education, talking to reporters on the 8th, said that the Ministry of Education ordered Wenfa colleges that are poorly run in various places to close down. Recently, there have been requests to expedite the closure or to postpone it, or to allow the establishment of science departments. In order to help students with their studies or to close down, a considerable amount of time is required, and the Ministry of Education can appropriately extend the time, but the closure must be completed by the end of this year. If there is an intention to wait and see, then mandatory measures will be taken. As for requests to convert to science departments, in this era of promoting production education, it cannot be said that it does not meet the need. However, the establishment of agricultural, engineering, and science colleges must have considerable start-up and recurring expenses, as well as sufficient equipment and excellent qualified personnel, before they can be established. The Ministry of Education must still examine its funding, equipment, and personnel to see if they meet the statutory standards as the basis for approval or disapproval.

Ministry of Education Explains Naming Questions of Elementary and Middle Schools 209

The Ning Xia Provincial Department of Education previously submitted a request to the Ministry of Education to explain questions about Article 11 of the Elementary School Regulations and Article 7 of the Middle School Regulations regarding naming questions of elementary and middle schools, in order to comply with them. The Ministry of Education issued instructions and explanations the day before yesterday, stating roughly as follows: According to the submitted request to explain the various points of naming questions of elementary and middle schools, the following are the individual explanations: (1) If the location of a provincial elementary school and a county elementary school are in the same place, such as in a certain district of a certain county, according to the provisions of Article 11 of the Elementary School Regulations, the provincial elementary school should be named after the county name, and the county elementary school should be named after the place name of the district. (2) The attached elementary school of the provincial normal school should be named "Attached Elementary School of a Certain Provincial Normal School." (3) Provincial middle schools and provincial elementary schools should be prefixed with the words "Certain Provincial," and county elementary schools should be prefixed with the words "Certain County." You should be informed.

Local News

Shanghai Children's Welfare Association Established 214

Pan, Director of the Bureau, and Four Others Elected as Standing Committee Members

Chen Ji Cheng and Others Appointed as Members of the Childcare Business Committee　　Will Manage the Reception and Education of Homeless Beggar Children

The Shanghai Children's Welfare Association held its inaugural meeting in the Shanghai Municipal Government Auditorium at 2:00 PM yesterday. The details are as follows:

The committee members present were Mayor Wu Tie Cheng (represented by Li Ting An), Director of the Education Bureau Pan Gong Zhan, Director of the Health Bureau Li Ting An, Director of the Public Security Bureau Wen Hong En (represented by Yin Guan San), Cai Hong Tian of the Municipal Party Department, Yang Zhi Hao of the Bar Association, Huang Zao Xiong of the Municipal Education Association, Hu Shu Yi of the Children's Morning News, Chen Song Chun of the Citizen Education Center, Wang Zhong Fu of the Chinese Women and Children Relief Association, Wang Bin Yan of the Zha Bei Charity Group, and expert committee members Wang Guan Yi, Zhu Shao Ping, Zhu Zi Qiao, Qiu Xi Sheng, Hu Shu Yi, Guo Shun, Chen Ji Cheng, Chen He Qin, Liu Wang Li Ming, and other twenty people.

Establishment Situation The meeting opened at 2:00 PM, and the mayor's representative Li Ting An was publicly elected as the temporary chairman, Hu Shu Yi was the recorder, Chen Song Chun was the master of ceremonies, and the ceremony was performed as usual. First, the chairman reported the meaning of forming this association and read the association's brief rules. Then, Director Pan of the Education Bureau reported on the preparations and the monthly recurring expense budget. Immediately, the standing committee members were elected, and the progress of the association affairs was discussed. The meeting was photographed and dismissed at around 4:00 PM.

Chairman's Report Chairman Li Ting An, representing Mayor Wu, reported that the purpose of the establishment of this association is to promote social attention to the status of children, develop children's businesses, and seek the happiness of all children in the city. Chinese children have always been in a harsh environment, and their status is very miserable. Such as forcing children to work, not paying attention to children's health, and trafficking abuse, and other harmful acts against children, are everywhere. As a result, the infant mortality rate is as high as three out of every thousand people, more than three times higher than in Europe and the United States. It must be known that today's children are the future masters of the country. If they are destroyed during the development period, they will not be able to become healthy citizens in the future, which will affect the future of the country, which is extremely serious. Therefore, after the establishment of this association, the colleagues of this association should do their work conscientiously and be responsible for protecting the happiness of children.

Shanghai Children's Welfare Association (Wang Kai Photography) 215

Preparation Process Next, Director Pan of the Education Bureau reported on the preparation process, saying that the motivation for initiating the organization of this association was that during the Children's Day held on April 4 this year, everyone felt that the development of children's undertakings could not be achieved by holding commemorative events on Children's Day. There must be a permanent agency to gradually seek the happiness of children. Therefore, the Education, Social, Health, and Public Security Bureaus were jointly responsible for preparing to organize the Municipal Children's Welfare Association and drafted brief rules that were submitted to the Municipal Government for record in mid-May. Also, in mid-June, in view of the difficulty of caring for children among the general factory workers, it initiated the organization of the Childcare Business Committee to prepare for the establishment of childcare centers. By mid-August, in accordance with the regulations, representatives of the national system and experts who were enthusiastic about children's undertakings were hired to serve as members of this association. It has been five months since the establishment so far. In the future, it is hoped that all members will work together to seek the happiness of all children in the city.

Election of Standing Committee After the report, the standing committee was elected. According to the association's brief rules, the number of standing committee members was fixed at five. However, all committee members agreed that five people were too few and unanimously agreed to increase it to seven. An election was held on the spot. As a result, the Director of the Education Bureau, the Child Welfare Association, the Director of the Health Bureau, the Children's Morning News, Chen He Qin and other five people were definitely elected as standing committee members. Hu Shu Yi and Liu Wang Li Ming had the next highest number of votes. When the number of standing committee members is submitted to the municipal government for approval to increase to seven, these second most members will become official standing committee members.

Matters for Discussion (1) The case where the address of this association should be temporarily stipulated was resolved to be temporarily located at the Municipal Education Bureau. (2) The case where the secretary of this association has already requested Zhou Wang He, please approve the recognition was resolved to be approved. (3) The case for ratifying the hiring of Feng Liu Tang, Yang Mao Rong, Gong Zi Yun, Yin Guan San, Hu Shu Yi, Chen Leng Seng, Chen Bai, Wu Li Guo, Jiang Jing Qing, Gao Jing Lang, Shen Tong, Wang Guan Yi, Chen Song Chun and other thirteen people as members of the Childcare Business Group Committee of this association was resolved to be approved. In addition, Liu Wang Li Ming, Qiu Xi Sheng, Mei Yun Ying, Chen Ji Cheng, etc. were recommended as members. (4) The case on the annual association affairs of this association was resolved to be that small committees should be set up in the Children's Protection Department, the Children's Health Department, the Children's Research Department, and the Children's Business Department of this association. Each committee will draft a business plan and submit it to the Standing Committee for review and then submit it to the General Assembly for approval. The Standing Committee will consider and appoint the candidates for each committee from the members of this association. (5) According to Article 4 of the Brief Rules of this Association, the method of raising temporary fees was resolved to be planned by the Standing Committee.

Motions (1) The case where the Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Children's Education Society, the Shanghai Women's Christian Association, and the Shanghai Branch of the China Educational Film Association were added as members of this association was resolved to be approved. (2) Liu Wang Li Ming proposed to seek to receive and educate homeless beggar children was resolved to be that the original proposer should provide opinions and submit them to the subcommittee. (3) Zhu Shao Ping proposed to solicit members to raise funds for this association, the opinion was that the original proposer should draft a plan and submit it to the Standing Committee. After the discussion, the meeting adjourned.

The Municipal Education Bureau Orders Vaccinations in Various Schools 216

Starting on the 15th of This Month

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau yesterday instructed the city's primary and secondary schools, saying that the Medical Bureau's letter stated that vaccination is the only good way to prevent smallpox. In accordance with the Ministry's orders, this bureau has organized free vaccinations in spring and autumn in the past. Now that the weather is cool in autumn, smallpox will be prevalent again. In order to maintain the health of all students, this bureau has decided to start vaccinations on the 15th of this month. However, the effective period of vaccination can last at least three years. All old students who have been vaccinated in the spring do not need to be vaccinated again. The vaccination schedule starts from the rural schools in the city, followed by the city schools in the urban area, and then the private registered schools and private unregistered schools. Therefore, in addition to replying to the letter, this order is hereby issued to inform the school.

Discovery by the Institute of Botany, National Peking Academy

The Mysterious Scenery of Plants on the Kunlun Mountains and Tibetan Plateau (Part 1) 223

Construction of Laboratories for Lower Plants and Cryptogams

Establishment of Nature Reserves and Return of Specimens from Xinjiang and Mongolia

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) The Institute of Botany of the National Peking Academy began preparations in September of the 18th year of the Republic of China, hiring Dr. Liu Shen'e as a part-time researcher and director of the Institute, and Dr. Lin Rong as a part-time researcher. Recently, Dr. Liu Zhen'e was changed to a full-time researcher and director, and Zhong Guangguang was hired as a full-time researcher. At the beginning of the preparations, the Institute selected Laiyuan Building in the Natural History Museum as the site, made some repairs, and started work. On the one hand, it engaged in collections near Beiping, and on the other hand, it sorted out specimens donated by various parties. Over the years, it has gradually expanded, increased equipment, carried out long-term and long-distance collections, and in addition to research work, in order to popularize biological knowledge, it has jointly established a botanical garden with the Natural History Museum to cultivate local and foreign plants for observation. The Institute currently has three researchers, five assistants, one draftsman, one botanical garden administrator, one trainee, one clerk, and one typist.

Construction and Equipment 224

Most of the funding for the Institute of Botany is used for collecting specimens and purchasing books, so it has not been able to expand in terms of construction. When the Institute's staff goes out to collect in the summer and autumn, it feels a little more spacious, but in the winter, many people live in one room, which is quite cramped. The existing buildings can be divided into the following five parts: (1) The research is located in Laiyuan Building, which has a total of twelve rooms. Except for two rooms that serve as passageways upstairs and downstairs, the rest are used for offices, libraries, and research. (2) The specimen room has fourteen main rooms, located south of Laiyuan Building. It was converted from the animal specimen room of the former agricultural experiment station and is still considered spacious. The four corridors are separated into multiple rooms, which are planned to be used for organizing specimens. (3) The botanical garden is jointly operated by the Institute of Botany and the Natural History Museum, covering an area of ​​about 40 acres. Local and foreign plants are cultivated according to classification order. Currently, about 700 species have been cultivated. (4) There are five storage rooms, which currently store heavy plant specimens. (5) There are currently fourteen staff rooms. As for the equipment of the Institute, the main points are as follows: (1) Instruments and books. The current work of the Institute focuses on the classification and distribution of Chinese plants, so all instruments are only for use and are very simple. There are only a few microscopes, cameras, etc. Specimen cabinets are gradually added, and there are currently 103 cabinets and more than 1,000 glass bottles. The Institute's books are currently mainly about seed plants, with more than 130 types. There are also several complete old magazines, which are not easy to buy. (2) Specimens. Except for a part that was donated and exchanged by local areas, the rest were collected by the Institute itself in the past two years. There are currently about 24,000 copies. Specimens have been collected from Hebei, Shanxi, Shandong, Henan, Chahar, Suiyuan, Gansu, Qinghai, Xinjiang, Liaoning, Jilin, Sichuan, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Guangdong and other provinces.

Future Plans 225

(1) Separate research rooms. The current research of the Institute of Botany focuses on the classification of higher plants due to practical needs, and lower plants are only taken care of with spare energy. However, moss, fungi, algae, and other things have a wide range, and their research methods are not entirely the same as those of higher plants, so the equipment is also different. It is planned to use the existing research rooms to specialize in the research of higher plants, and build new houses to establish research rooms for lower plants, cryptogams, or cryptogams." Researching biology should not focus solely on indoor work, but should seek to be close to nature and personally observe the phenomenon of plant growth in the wild. This kind of work cannot be effective with short-term collections. In European and American countries, research rooms are often established in the wild due to special local conditions, so that long-term field investigations can be carried out. The Institute also intends to follow this idea and establish a high-mountain plant research room near Beiping or in a farther place. (2) Add books and instruments. The Institute's collection of books is not sufficient, and it is inconvenient to travel back and forth to various libraries in Beiping City when consulting books in the suburbs. Therefore, it has recently been trying to purchase books. As for instruments, since it is planned to set up separate research rooms, there are many that still need to be added. (3) Establish natural protected areas. All things in nature live together, compete for growth and thrive. Every time human intervention is implemented, the face is changed, or it is completely destroyed. Rare species are even extinct, which is very sad. Therefore, European and American countries all have natural protected areas. Within the area, the growth and decline of organisms are left to nature. Chinese people often do not care about this. For example, the few remaining small forests near Beiping have been severely cut down in recent years. In a few years, they will all become bald mountains and ridges, without any green. The Institute also intends to pay attention to this aspect this time, or to establish a natural protected area on its own, and set up a research room in it. (4) Promote botanical gardens. The establishment of botanical gardens is not only for social observation,

teaching materials for schools, but also to preserve living specimens for reference during research. Even in plant taxonomy, there are often problems that need to be solved by observing plant growth. In addition to planning to promote the original botanical garden, the Institute also plans to select a suitable location in the Natural History Museum to set up a forest garden and build another greenhouse. In addition, the Institute has transported back many seeds from Xinjiang, Mongolia, and other places, and has long planned to establish a border plant garden, but it has not been able to implement it due to limited funding. In addition to the above-mentioned botanical garden, forest garden, and border plant garden, it is also planned to open an experimental field for research purposes. (To be continued)
